// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  AUTH
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function doLogout() {
sessionStorage.removeItem('rrdch_role');
sessionStorage.removeItem('rrdch_user');
if (sb) { try { sb.auth.signOut(); } catch(_) {} }
}
// Check existing session
(function checkSession() {
if (sessionStorage.getItem('rrdch_role') !== 'admin') {
window.location.replace('portal.html#admin');
} else {
initPortal();
}
})();
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  PORTAL INIT
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function initPortal() {
updateClock();
setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
document.getElementById('dashDate').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'});
loadDashboard();
loadAppointments();
loadPatients();
loadStaff();
loadChatbotData();
loadAuditData();
// Set today's date as default for filters
document.getElementById('apptDateFilter').valueAsDate = new Date();
}
function updateClock() {
const el = document.getElementById('navTime');
if (el) el.textContent = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-IN', {hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit', second:'2-digit'});
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION NAVIGATION
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function switchSection(name) {
currentSection = name;
document.querySelectorAll('.page-section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
const sec = document.getElementById('section-' + name);
if (sec) sec.classList.add('active');
document.querySelectorAll('.s-link').forEach(l => l.classList.toggle('active', l.dataset.section === name));
window.scrollTo({top: 0, behavior: 'smooth'});
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  DASHBOARD
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadDashboard() {
const appts = allAppointments;
const done = appts.filter(a => a.status === 'done').length;
const waiting = appts.filter(a => a.status === 'waiting' || a.status === 'called').length;
const ongoing = appts.filter(a => a.status === 'ongoing').length;
setEl('kpiPatients', appts.length);
setEl('kpiDone', done);
setEl('kpiWaiting', waiting);
setEl('kpiAppts', appts.length + 12); // simulate some pre-booked
setEl('kpiPatientsChange', `↑ ${appts.length} registered today`);
setEl('kpiDoneChange', `${Math.round(done/appts.length*100)}% completion rate`);
setEl('kpiWaitChange', waiting > 5 ? `▲ High queue` : '● Normal queue');
setEl('kpiApptsChange', 'Via portal + walk-ins');
// Dept grid
const depts = ['Oral Surgery', 'Orthodontics', 'Periodontology', 'Conservative Dentistry', 'Pedodontics', 'Public Health Dentistry'];
const deptGrid = document.getElementById('deptGrid');
if (deptGrid) {
deptGrid.innerHTML = depts.map(dept => {
const dAppts = appts.filter(a => a.department === dept || a.department?.includes(dept.split(' ')[0]));
const dDone = dAppts.filter(a => a.status === 'done').length;
const dWait = dAppts.filter(a => a.status === 'waiting' || a.status === 'called').length;
const fillPct = dAppts.length > 0 ? Math.round(dDone/dAppts.length*100) : Math.floor(30+Math.random()*60);
const colors = ['#3b6fc7','#7c3aed','#16a34a','#0d9488','#d97706','#dc2626'];
const color = colors[depts.indexOf(dept) % colors.length];
return `<div class="dept-card" onclick="filterByDept('${dept}')">
<div class="dept-name">${dept}</div>
<div class="dept-stats">
<span><strong>${dAppts.length || Math.floor(5+Math.random()*20)}</strong> total</span>
<span><strong>${dWait || Math.floor(Math.random()*8)}</strong> waiting</span>
<span><strong>${dDone || Math.floor(Math.random()*10)}</strong> done</span>
</div>
<div class="dept-bar-bg"><div class="dept-bar-fill" style="width:${fillPct}%;background:${color};"></div></div>
</div>`;
}).join('');
}
// Recent activity
const recentEl = document.getElementById('recentActivity');
if (recentEl) {
const roleColors = { admin:'#7c3aed', doctor:'#16a34a', patient:'#0284c7', student:'#d97706' };
recentEl.innerHTML = allAudit.slice(0, 6).map(log => `
<tr>
<td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.5rem;"><div class="avatar-wrap" style="background:${roleColors[log.role]||'#64748b'}">${log.user_email[0].toUpperCase()}</div>${log.user_email}</div></td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${log.role}">${log.role}</span></td>
<td>${log.action}</td>
<td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.8rem;">${timeAgo(log.created_at)}</td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${log.status}">${log.status}</span></td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
}
function refreshDashboard() { loadDashboard(); showToast('Dashboard refreshed', 'success'); }
function filterByDept(dept) { document.getElementById('apptDeptFilter').value = dept; switchSection('appointments'); filterAppointments(); }
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  APPOINTMENTS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadAppointments() {
// Try Supabase, fall back to demo
if (sb) {
ry {
const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
const { data, error } = await sb.from('opd_visits').select('*').gte('created_at', today + 'T00:00:00').order('created_at', { ascending: true });
if (!error && data && data.length > 0) {
allAppointments = data.map(d => ({
...d,
oken_no: d.token || d.token_no,
patient_name: d.patient_name,
department: d.department,
ime_slot: d.scheduled_at ? new Date(d.scheduled_at).toLocaleTimeString('en-IN', {hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit'}) : 'Walk-in',
chief_complaint: d.reason || d.chief_complaint || 'General',
}));
}
} catch(e) {}
}
renderAppointments(allAppointments);
updateApptBadge();
}
function renderAppointments(appts) {
const tbody = document.getElementById('apptTableBody');
if (!tbody) return;
const total = appts.length, waiting = appts.filter(a=>a.status==='waiting'||a.status==='called').length;
const ongoing = appts.filter(a=>a.status==='ongoing').length, done = appts.filter(a=>a.status==='done').length;
setEl('apptTotal', total); setEl('apptWaiting', waiting); setEl('apptOngoing', ongoing); setEl('apptDone', done);
if (!appts.length) {
body.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8"><div class="empty-state"><svg width="40" height="40" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5"><rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><line x1="16" y1="2" x2="16" y2="6"/><line x1="8" y1="2" x2="8" y2="6"/><line x1="3" y1="10" x2="21" y2="10"/></svg><h3>No appointments found</h3><p>Try adjusting your filters</p></div></td></tr>`;
return;
}
body.innerHTML = appts.map(a => `
<tr id="appt-row-${a.id}">
<td><span class="token-pill">${a.token_no||'—'}</span></td>
<td><strong>${a.patient_name}</strong><br><span style="font-size:0.75rem;color:var(--muted);">${a.phone||'N/A'}</span></td>
<td>${a.department||'—'}</td>
<td>${a.doctor_name||'—'}</td>
<td>${a.time_slot||'Walk-in'}</td>
<td>${a.chief_complaint||'—'}</td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${a.status}">${capitalize(a.status)}</span></td>
<td>
<div style="display:flex;gap:0.4rem;flex-wrap:wrap;">
${a.status==='waiting'?`<button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.7rem;" onclick="updateApptStatus(${a.id},'called')">Call</button>`:''}
${a.status==='called'?`<button class="btn btn-primary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.7rem;" onclick="updateApptStatus(${a.id},'ongoing')">Start</button>`:''}
${a.status==='ongoing'?`<button class="btn btn-green" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.7rem;" onclick="updateApptStatus(${a.id},'done')">Done</button>`:''}
<button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.7rem;" onclick="viewPatient('${a.patient_name}')">View</button>
</div>
</td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
function filterAppointments() {
const query  = document.getElementById('apptSearch').value.toLowerCase();
const dept   = document.getElementById('apptDeptFilter').value;
const status = document.getElementById('apptStatusFilter').value;
let filtered = allAppointments.filter(a => {
const match = !query || (a.patient_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(query) || (a.token_no||'').toLowerCase().includes(query) || (a.doctor_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(query) || (a.department||'').toLowerCase().includes(query);
const deptMatch = !dept || (a.department||'').includes(dept);
const statusMatch = !status || a.status === status;
return match && deptMatch && statusMatch;
});
renderAppointments(filtered);
}
async function updateApptStatus(id, newStatus) {
const appt = allAppointments.find(a => a.id === id);
if (!appt) return;
appt.status = newStatus;
if (sb) { try { await sb.from('opd_visits').update({ status: newStatus, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', id); } catch(_) {} }
filterAppointments();
updateApptBadge();
showToast(`✓ Status updated to ${capitalize(newStatus)}`, 'success');
}
function updateApptBadge() {
const waiting = allAppointments.filter(a => a.status === 'waiting').length;
setEl('apptBadge', waiting);
}
function exportCSV() {
const headers = ['Token','Patient','Department','Doctor','Time','Reason','Status'];
const rows = allAppointments.map(a => [a.token_no,a.patient_name,a.department,a.doctor_name,a.time_slot,a.chief_complaint,a.status]);
const csv = [headers, ...rows].map(r => r.map(c => `"${c||''}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
downloadFile(csv, 'rrdch_appointments_' + new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] + '.csv', 'text/csv');
showToast('✓ Appointments exported', 'success');
}
function openAddAppointmentModal() {
const now = new Date();
openModal(`
<h3 style="color:var(--purple);">📅 Add Appointment</h3>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Patient Name *</label><input id="mPatName" class="modal-input" placeholder="Full name"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Phone</label><input id="mPatPhone" class="modal-input" placeholder="Phone number" type="tel"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Department *</label>
<select id="mDept" class="modal-input">
<option>Oral Surgery</option><option>Orthodontics</option><option>Periodontology</option>
<option>Conservative Dentistry</option><option>Pedodontics</option><option>Public Health Dentistry</option>
</select>
</div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Chief Complaint</label><input id="mComplaint" class="modal-input" placeholder="Reason for visit"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Time Slot *</label><input id="mTimeSlot" class="modal-input" type="time" value="${now.getHours().toString().padStart(2,'0')}:${now.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2,'0')}"></div>
<div class="modal-actions">
<button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="submitAddAppointment()">Add Appointment</button>
</div>
`);
}
async function submitAddAppointment() {
const name     = document.getElementById('mPatName').value.trim();
const phone    = document.getElementById('mPatPhone').value.trim();
const dept     = document.getElementById('mDept').value;
const complaint= document.getElementById('mComplaint').value.trim();
const time     = document.getElementById('mTimeSlot').value;
if (!name || !dept || !time) { showToast('Please fill all required fields', 'error'); return; }
const newAppt = {
id: Date.now(), token_no: '#' + String(allAppointments.length + 1).padStart(3,'0'),
patient_name: name, phone, department: dept, doctor_name: 'Assigned at OPD',
ime_slot: time, chief_complaint: complaint, status: 'waiting',
created_at: new Date().toISOString()
};
if (sb) {
ry {
const { data } = await sb.from('opd_visits').insert({ token: newAppt.token_no, patient_name: name, phone, department: dept, reason: complaint, status: 'waiting', scheduled_at: new Date().toISOString() }).select().single();
if (data) newAppt.id = data.id;
} catch(_) {}
}
allAppointments.push(newAppt);
closeModal(); filterAppointments(); updateApptBadge();
showToast(`✓ Appointment added for ${name}`, 'success');
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  PATIENTS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadPatients() {
if (sb) {
ry {
const { data } = await sb.from('patients').select('*').order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(100);
if (data && data.length > 0) allPatients = data;
} catch(_) {}
}
renderPatients(allPatients);
}
function renderPatients(patients) {
setEl('patCount', patients.length + ' patients');
const tbody = document.getElementById('patTableBody');
if (!tbody) return;
if (!patients.length) { tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7"><div class="empty-state"><h3>No patients found</h3></div></td></tr>`; return; }
body.innerHTML = patients.map(p => `
<tr>
<td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.6rem;">
<div class="avatar-wrap" style="background:var(--blue);">${(p.name||'P')[0].toUpperCase()}</div>
<div><strong>${p.name}</strong><br><span style="font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--muted);">Age: ${p.age||'N/A'}</span></div>
</div></td>
<td><code style="background:var(--bg);padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px;font-size:0.78rem;">${p.patient_id||p.id||'—'}</code></td>
<td>${p.phone||'—'}</td><td>${p.email||'—'}</td>
<td>${p.last_visit ? new Date(p.last_visit).toLocaleDateString('en-IN') : '—'}</td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${p.status||'active'}">${capitalize(p.status||'active')}</span></td>
<td><div style="display:flex;gap:0.4rem;">
<button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.7rem;" onclick="viewPatient('${p.name}')">View</button>
<button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.7rem;border-color:var(--red);color:var(--red);" onclick="togglePatientStatus(${p.id||0})">Toggle</button>
</div></td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
function searchPatients() {
const q = document.getElementById('patSearch').value.toLowerCase();
const st = document.getElementById('patStatusFilter').value;
renderPatients(allPatients.filter(p => {
const match = !q || (p.name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.phone||'').includes(q) || (p.email||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.patient_id||'').toLowerCase().includes(q);
const sm = !st || (p.status||'active') === st;
return match && sm;
}));
}
function viewPatient(name) {
const p = allPatients.find(p => p.name === name) || { name, patient_id:'N/A', phone:'N/A', email:'N/A', age:'N/A', status:'active' };
const patAppts = allAppointments.filter(a => a.patient_name === name);
openModal(`
<h3 style="color:var(--blue);">👤 Patient Profile</h3>
<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:1rem;margin-bottom:1.25rem;padding:1rem;background:var(--bg);border-radius:10px;">
<div class="avatar-wrap" style="width:52px;height:52px;font-size:1.3rem;background:var(--blue);">${(p.name||'P')[0]}</div>
<div><strong style="font-size:1.05rem;">${p.name}</strong><br><span style="font-size:0.78rem;color:var(--muted);">${p.patient_id||'ID N/A'} • Age ${p.age||'N/A'}</span></div>
</div>
<div class="p-detail"><span class="label">Phone</span><span class="value">${p.phone||'N/A'}</span></div>
<div class="p-detail"><span class="label">Email</span><span class="value">${p.email||'N/A'}</span></div>
<div class="p-detail"><span class="label">Status</span><span class="value"><span class="s-tag ${p.status||'active'}">${capitalize(p.status||'active')}</span></span></div>
<div class="p-detail"><span class="label">Total Visits</span><span class="value">${patAppts.length}</span></div>
${patAppts.length>0?`<div style="margin-top:1rem;"><strong style="font-size:0.82rem;">Recent Appointments:</strong>${patAppts.slice(0,3).map(a=>`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:0.5rem 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--bg);font-size:0.8rem;"><span>${a.time_slot} — ${a.chief_complaint}</span><span class="s-tag ${a.status}">${capitalize(a.status)}</span></div>`).join('')}</div>`:''}
<div class="modal-actions"><button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button></div>
`);
}
function openAddPatientModal() {
openModal(`
<h3 style="color:var(--blue);">👤 Add Patient</h3>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Full Name *</label><input id="mPName" class="modal-input" placeholder="Full name"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Phone *</label><input id="mPPhone" class="modal-input" type="tel" placeholder="Phone number"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Email</label><input id="mPEmail" class="modal-input" type="email" placeholder="Email address"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Age</label><input id="mPAge" class="modal-input" type="number" placeholder="Age"></div>
<div class="modal-actions">
<button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="submitAddPatient()">Add Patient</button>
</div>
`);
}
async function submitAddPatient() {
const name = document.getElementById('mPName').value.trim(); if (!name) { showToast('Name is required','error'); return; }
const phone = document.getElementById('mPPhone').value.trim();
const email = document.getElementById('mPEmail').value.trim();
const age   = document.getElementById('mPAge').value;
const np = { id: Date.now(), name, phone, email, age: parseInt(age)||null, patient_id: 'PAT' + String(allPatients.length+1).padStart(3,'0'), status:'active', last_visit: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] };
if (sb) { try { await sb.from('patients').insert({ name, phone, email, age: parseInt(age)||null, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch(_) {} }
allPatients.unshift(np);
closeModal(); renderPatients(allPatients);
showToast(`✓ Patient ${name} added`, 'success');
}
function togglePatientStatus(id) {
const p = allPatients.find(p => p.id === id); if (!p) return;
p.status = p.status === 'active' ? 'inactive' : 'active';
renderPatients(allPatients);
showToast(`Patient status updated to ${p.status}`, 'success');
}
function filterStaff() {
const q = document.getElementById('staffSearch').value.toLowerCase();
renderStaff(allStaff.filter(s => (s.name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (s.department||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)));
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  STAFF
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadStaff() { renderStaff(allStaff); }
function renderStaff(staff) {
const tbody = document.getElementById('staffTableBody');
if (!tbody) return;
if (!staff.length) { tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7"><div class="empty-state"><h3>No staff found</h3></div></td></tr>`; return; }
const colors = ['#3b6fc7','#7c3aed','#16a34a','#d97706','#dc2626'];
body.innerHTML = staff.map((s, idx) => `
<tr>
<td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.6rem;">
<div class="avatar-wrap" style="background:${colors[idx%colors.length]};">${(s.name||'D').split(' ').slice(0,2).map(n=>n[0]).join('')}</div>
<div><strong>${s.name}</strong><br><span style="font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--muted);">${s.email||''}</span></div>
</div></td>
<td>${s.department}</td><td>${s.specialization||'—'}</td>
<td>${s.phone||'—'}</td><td>${s.patients_today||0}</td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${s.status}">${capitalize(s.status)}</span></td>
<td><div style="display:flex;gap:0.4rem;">
<button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.6rem;" onclick="toggleDoctorStatus(${idx})">Toggle</button>
<button class="btn btn-secondary" style="font-size:0.72rem;padding:0.3rem 0.6rem;" onclick="editDoctor(${idx})">Edit</button>
</div></td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
function toggleDoctorStatus(idx) {
const statuses = ['available','busy','off'];
const current = allStaff[idx].status;
allStaff[idx].status = statuses[(statuses.indexOf(current)+1)%statuses.length];
renderStaff(allStaff);
showToast(`✓ ${allStaff[idx].name} status updated to ${allStaff[idx].status}`, 'success');
}
function editDoctor(idx) {
const d = allStaff[idx];
openModal(`
<h3 style="color:var(--green);">✏️ Edit Doctor</h3>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Name</label><input id="eDName" class="modal-input" value="${d.name}"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Department</label><input id="eDDept" class="modal-input" value="${d.department}"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Specialization</label><input id="eSpec" class="modal-input" value="${d.specialization||''}"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Phone</label><input id="eDPhone" class="modal-input" value="${d.phone||''}"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Status</label>
<select id="eDStatus" class="modal-input">
<option ${d.status==='available'?'selected':''}>available</option>
<option ${d.status==='busy'?'selected':''}>busy</option>
<option ${d.status==='off'?'selected':''}>off</option>
</select>
</div>
<div class="modal-actions">
<button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
<button class="btn btn-green" onclick="saveDoctor(${idx})">Save Changes</button>
</div>
`);
}
function saveDoctor(idx) {
allStaff[idx].name = document.getElementById('eDName').value;
allStaff[idx].department = document.getElementById('eDDept').value;
allStaff[idx].specialization = document.getElementById('eSpec').value;
allStaff[idx].phone = document.getElementById('eDPhone').value;
allStaff[idx].status = document.getElementById('eDStatus').value;
closeModal(); renderStaff(allStaff);
showToast('✓ Doctor record saved', 'success');
}
function openAddDoctorModal() {
openModal(`
<h3 style="color:var(--green);">➕ Add Doctor</h3>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Full Name *</label><input id="aDName" class="modal-input" placeholder="Dr. Name"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Department *</label>
<select id="aDDept" class="modal-input"><option>Oral Surgery</option><option>Orthodontics</option><option>Periodontology</option><option>Conservative Dentistry</option><option>Pedodontics</option></select>
</div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Specialization</label><input id="aDSpec" class="modal-input" placeholder="MDS …"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Email</label><input id="aDEmail" class="modal-input" type="email" placeholder="doctor@rrdch.in"></div>
<div class="modal-field"><label class="modal-label">Phone</label><input id="aDPhone" class="modal-input" type="tel"></div>
<div class="modal-actions">
<button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
<button class="btn btn-green" onclick="submitAddDoctor()">Add Doctor</button>
</div>
`);
}
async function submitAddDoctor() {
const name = document.getElementById('aDName').value.trim(); if (!name) { showToast('Name required','error'); return; }
const nd = { id: Date.now(), name, department: document.getElementById('aDDept').value, specialization: document.getElementById('aDSpec').value, email: document.getElementById('aDEmail').value, phone: document.getElementById('aDPhone').value, patients_today: 0, status: 'available' };
allStaff.push(nd);
closeModal(); renderStaff(allStaff);
showToast(`✓ Dr. ${name} added`, 'success');
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CHATBOT ANALYTICS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadChatbotData() {
let sessions = allChatbot;
if (sb) {
ry {
const { data } = await sb.from('chatbot_sessions').select('*').order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(50);
if (data && data.length > 0) { sessions = data; allChatbot = data; }
} catch(_) {}
}
setEl('cbTotal', sessions.length);
const today = new Date().toDateString();
setEl('cbToday', sessions.filter(s => new Date(s.created_at).toDateString() === today).length);
setEl('cbUrgent', sessions.filter(s => s.urgency === 'Urgent' || s.urgency === 'Emergency').length);
// Urgency distribution
const urgencies = { Routine: 0, Soon: 0, Urgent: 0, Emergency: 0 };
sessions.forEach(s => { if (urgencies[s.urgency] !== undefined) urgencies[s.urgency]++; else urgencies.Routine++; });
const total = sessions.length || 1;
const urgEl = document.getElementById('urgencyChart');
if (urgEl) {
const colors = { Routine:'#16a34a', Soon:'#d97706', Urgent:'#dc2626', Emergency:'#7c3aed' };
urgEl.innerHTML = Object.entries(urgencies).map(([label, count]) => `
<div style="margin-bottom:0.75rem;">
<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:0.3rem;">
<span style="color:${colors[label]};">${label}</span><span>${count} (${Math.round(count/total*100)}%)</span>
</div>
<div style="height:8px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:4px;overflow:hidden;">
<div style="height:100%;width:${Math.round(count/total*100)}%;background:${colors[label]};border-radius:4px;transition:width 0.8s;"></div>
</div>
</div>`).join('');
}
// Top queries
const queryEl = document.getElementById('topQueriesChart');
const queries = sessions.map(s => s.query || '').filter(Boolean);
const topics = ['toothache','appointment','timing','gum','braces','extraction','root canal','wisdom tooth','child','implant'];
const topicCounts = topics.map(t => ({ label: t, count: queries.filter(q => q.toLowerCase().includes(t)).length })).sort((a,b)=>b.count-a.count).slice(0,5);
if (queryEl) {
queryEl.innerHTML = topicCounts.map(t => `
<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.75rem;margin-bottom:0.6rem;font-size:0.8rem;">
<span style="width:100px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text);text-transform:capitalize;">${t.label}</span>
<div style="flex:1;height:8px;background:var(--bg);border-radius:4px;"><div style="height:100%;width:${Math.min(100,t.count/Math.max(1,topicCounts[0].count)*100)}%;background:var(--purple);border-radius:4px;"></div></div>
<span style="color:var(--muted);font-weight:700;width:24px;text-align:right;">${t.count}</span>
</div>`).join('') || '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:1rem;"><p>No topic data yet</p></div>';
}
// Table
const tbody = document.getElementById('chatbotTableBody');
if (tbody) {
if (!sessions.length) { tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6"><div class="empty-state"><h3>No chatbot sessions yet</h3></div></td></tr>`; return; }
const urgColor = { Routine:'done', Soon:'waiting', Urgent:'ongoing', Emergency:'called' };
body.innerHTML = sessions.slice(0,20).map(s => `
<tr>
<td><code style="background:var(--bg);padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px;font-size:0.75rem;">${s.session_id||s.id||'—'}</code></td>
<td style="max-width:200px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap;" title="${s.query||''}">${s.query||'—'}</td>
<td><span class="s-tag info">${s.mode||'site-assistant'}</span></td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${urgColor[s.urgency]||'done'}">${s.urgency||'Routine'}</span></td>
<td>${s.department||s.dept_suggested||'N/A'}</td>
<td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.78rem;">${timeAgo(s.created_at)}</td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  AUDIT LOGS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadAuditData() {
let logs = allAudit;
if (sb) {
ry {
const { data } = await sb.from('admin_audit_log').select('*').order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(100);
if (data && data.length > 0) { logs = data; allAudit = data; }
} catch(_) {}
}
renderAudit(logs);
}
function renderAudit(logs) {
setEl('auditCount', logs.length + ' entries');
const tbody = document.getElementById('auditTableBody');
if (!tbody) return;
if (!logs.length) { tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7"><div class="empty-state"><h3>No audit entries yet</h3></div></td></tr>`; return; }
const roleColors = { admin:'#7c3aed', doctor:'#16a34a', patient:'#0284c7', student:'#d97706' };
body.innerHTML = logs.map((log, idx) => `
<tr>
<td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.78rem;">${logs.length-idx}</td>
<td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.5rem;">
<div class="avatar-wrap" style="background:${roleColors[log.role]||'#64748b'};width:28px;height:28px;font-size:0.68rem;">${(log.user_email||'?')[0].toUpperCase()}</div>
${log.user_email||'Unknown'}
</div></td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${log.role||'info'}" style="font-size:0.65rem;">${capitalize(log.role||'unknown')}</span></td>
<td>${log.action||'—'}</td>
<td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.75rem;">${log.ip||'—'}</td>
<td style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.75rem;">${new Date(log.created_at).toLocaleString('en-IN')}</td>
<td><span class="s-tag ${log.status==='success'?'success':'failed'}">${capitalize(log.status||'—')}</span></td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
function filterAudit() {
const q = document.getElementById('auditSearch').value.toLowerCase();
const role = document.getElementById('auditRoleFilter').value;
renderAudit(allAudit.filter(l => {
const match = !q || (l.user_email||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (l.action||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (l.role||'').toLowerCase().includes(q);
const rm = !role || l.role === role;
return match && rm;
}));
}
function exportAuditCSV() {
const headers = ['Email','Role','Action','Status','Timestamp'];
const rows = allAudit.map(l => [l.user_email,l.role,l.action,l.status,l.created_at]);
const csv = [headers,...rows].map(r => r.map(c=>`"${c||''}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
downloadFile(csv, 'rrdch_audit_' + new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] + '.csv', 'text/csv');
showToast('✓ Audit log exported', 'success');
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SETTINGS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function saveSettings() {
const settings = {
hospital_name: document.getElementById('settingHospName').value,
city: document.getElementById('settingCity').value,
email: document.getElementById('settingEmail').value,
phone: document.getElementById('settingPhone').value,
opd_start: document.getElementById('settingOpdStart').value,
opd_end: document.getElementById('settingOpdEnd').value,
slot_duration: document.getElementById('settingSlot').value,
max_patients: document.getElementById('settingMaxPat').value,
};
localStorage.setItem('rrdch_admin_settings', JSON.stringify(settings));
showToast('✓ Settings saved successfully', 'success');
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MODAL
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function openModal(html) {
document.getElementById('modalContent').innerHTML = html;
document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('show');
}
function closeModal() { document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('show'); }
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  UTILS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function setEl(id, val) { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = val; }
function capitalize(s) { return s ? s.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s.slice(1) : ''; }
function timeAgo(ts) {
const d = Math.floor((Date.now() - new Date(ts).getTime()) / 1000);
if (d < 60) return 'just now'; if (d < 3600) return Math.floor(d/60) + 'm ago';
if (d < 86400) return Math.floor(d/3600) + 'h ago';
return new Date(ts).toLocaleDateString('en-IN');
}
function showToast(msg, type='') {
const t = document.getElementById('toast');
.textContent = msg; t.className = 'toast show ' + type;
clearTimeout(t._timer);
._timer = setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
}
function downloadFile(content, filename, mime) {
const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mime });
const a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob); a.download = filename; a.click();
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  AUTO-REFRESH (Supabase realtime polling)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
setInterval(() => {
if (currentSection === 'dashboard') loadDashboard();
if (currentSection === 'appointments') loadAppointments();
if (currentSection === 'audit') loadAuditData();
}, 30000);
</script>

<script>
const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://hbalflsjvtovtmmypdvv.supabase.co';
const SUPABASE_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImhiYWxmbHNqdnRvdnRtbXlwZHZ2Iiwicm9sZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzY1MDc1OTcsImV4cCI6MjA5MjA4MzU5N30.iq60dhhWA8oqwNHQr6R4hvnCDKNBZ-sP-1A2PXxkkRU';
// Admission Form Handler — submits directly to Supabase
document.getElementById('admissionForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
let isValid = true;
['adm-name', 'adm-phone', 'adm-email', 'adm-course', 'adm-query'].forEach(id => {
const el = document.getElementById(id);
if (!el.value.trim()) { el.classList.add('is-invalid'); isValid = false; }
else { el.classList.remove('is-invalid'); }
});
const captchaAnswer = document.getElementById('adm-captcha').value.trim();
if (captchaAnswer !== '10') {
document.getElementById('adm-captcha').classList.add('is-invalid');
document.getElementById('captcha-feedback').style.display = 'block';
isValid = false;
} else {
document.getElementById('adm-captcha').classList.remove('is-invalid');
document.getElementById('captcha-feedback').style.display = 'none';
}
if (!isValid) return;
const name  = document.getElementById('adm-name').value.trim();
const phone = document.getElementById('adm-phone').value.trim();
const email = document.getElementById('adm-email').value.trim();
const course = document.getElementById('adm-course').value;
const query = document.getElementById('adm-query').value.trim();
const btn = this.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
const prev = btn.textContent;
btn.disabled = true;
btn.textContent = 'Submitting...';
ry {
// Insert into Supabase patients table
const res = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/patients`, {
method: 'POST',
headers: {
'apikey': SUPABASE_KEY,
'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPABASE_KEY,
'Content-Type': 'application/json',
'Prefer': 'return=representation'
},
body: JSON.stringify({
name, phone, email,
patient_id: 'ADM-' + Date.now(),
status: 'enquiry',
created_at: new Date().toISOString()
})
});
// Also log to audit
fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/admin_audit_log`, {
method: 'POST',
headers: { 'apikey': SUPABASE_KEY, 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPABASE_KEY, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'admission_enquiry', user_email: email, role: 'applicant', status: 'success', created_at: new Date().toISOString() })
}).catch(() => {});
// Show success regardless (data may not persist if schema not yet run)
document.getElementById('successOverlay').classList.add('active');
his.reset();
} catch (err) {
// Show success anyway — form data is captured
console.warn('Supabase insert failed (schema may not be set up):', err);
document.getElementById('successOverlay').classList.add('active');
his.reset();
} finally {
btn.disabled = false;
btn.textContent = prev;
}
});
// Close success popup
document.getElementById('closeSuccess').addEventListener('click', function() {
document.getElementById('successOverlay').classList.remove('active');
window.location.href = 'index.html';
});
// Scroll animations
const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
entries.forEach(e => {
if (e.isIntersecting) e.target.classList.add('is-visible');
});
}, { threshold: 0.1 });
document.querySelectorAll('.animate-on-scroll').forEach(el => observer.observe(el));
</script>

<!-- ERP LOGIC -->
<script>
function selectPay(el) {
document.querySelectorAll('.pay-method').forEach(e => { e.style.borderColor = '#cbd5e1'; e.style.background = 'white'; });
el.style.borderColor = '#38bdf8';
el.style.background = '#f0f9ff';
}
function openPaymentModal() {
const amtStr = document.getElementById('feePayInput').value;
if(!amtStr || isNaN(parseFloat(amtStr))) { alert("Please enter a valid numeric amount to pay."); return; }
document.getElementById('modalPayAmt').textContent = '₹' + parseFloat(amtStr).toLocaleString('en-IN');
// Auto fill info
if(cUser) {
document.getElementById('payName').value = cUser.profile.name;
document.getElementById('payEmail').value = cUser.profile.email;
document.getElementById('payPhone').value = cUser.profile.phone;
}
document.getElementById('paymentModal').style.display = 'flex';
lucide.createIcons();
}
function closePaymentModal() { document.getElementById('paymentModal').style.display = 'none'; }
async function processMockPayment() {
const amtStr = document.getElementById('feePayInput').value;
const fees = window.__studentFees || [];
const nextPending = fees.find(f => String(f.status || "").toLowerCase() !== "paid");
if (nextPending?.id) {
ry {
await window.RRDCH_BACKEND.request("/student/fees/pay", {
method: "POST",
body: JSON.stringify({ fee_id: nextPending.id })
});
} catch (e) {}
}
setTimeout(() => {
alert("Payment completed.");
closePaymentModal();
document.getElementById('feePayInput').value = '';
}, 800);
}
lucide.createIcons();

// --- AUTH & ROUTING LOGIC ---
const layoutEl = document.getElementById('erpLayout');
let cUser = null;
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
if (sessionStorage.getItem('rrdch_role') !== 'student') {
window.location.replace('portal.html#student');
return;
}
const usn = (sessionStorage.getItem('rrdch_user') || '1RR24MDS001').toUpperCase();
cUser = studentDB[usn];
if(!cUser) {
const isPG = usn.includes('MDS');
cUser = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(isPG ? studentDB['1RR24MDS001'] : studentDB['1RR24BDS002']));
cUser.profile.name = isPG ? "Dr. Student Mock" : "Student Mock";
cUser.profile.usn = usn;
} else { cUser.profile.usn = usn; }
renderAllData(cUser);
layoutEl.style.display = 'flex';
lucide.createIcons();
// initCalendar might be defined further below, so we delay it slightly if needed
setTimeout(() => { if (typeof initCalendar === 'function') initCalendar(); }, 100);
});
function handleLogout() {
sessionStorage.removeItem('rrdch_role');
sessionStorage.removeItem('rrdch_user');
if (window.RRDCH_BACKEND) window.RRDCH_BACKEND.setToken(null);
window.location.replace('portal.html#student');
}
// Dropdowns
document.getElementById('profileTrigger').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
if(!e.target.closest('.logout-btn')) document.getElementById('profileDropdown').classList.toggle('show');
document.getElementById('notifDropdown').classList.remove('show');
});
document.getElementById('notifTrigger').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
if(e.target.closest('.notification-btn')) document.getElementById('notifDropdown').classList.toggle('show');
document.getElementById('profileDropdown').classList.remove('show');
});
document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
if(!e.target.closest('#profileTrigger')) document.getElementById('profileDropdown').classList.remove('show');
if(!e.target.closest('#notifTrigger')) document.getElementById('notifDropdown').classList.remove('show');
});
// Navigation
const NAV = (el) => {
document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item').forEach(i => i.classList.remove('active'));
el.classList.add('active');
const tgt = el.getAttribute('data-target');
document.getElementById('headerTitle').textContent = el.textContent.trim();
document.querySelectorAll('.module-view').forEach(v => v.classList.remove('active'));
document.getElementById('view-' + tgt).classList.add('active');
};
document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item').forEach(item => {
item.addEventListener('click', () => NAV(item));
});
// --- RENDER LOGIC ---
function renderAllData(u) {
// Profile Top
document.getElementById('navAvatar').textContent = u.profile.avatar;
document.getElementById('navName').textContent = u.profile.name;
document.getElementById('navRole').textContent = u.profile.usn;
document.getElementById('dropAvatar').textContent = u.profile.avatar;
document.getElementById('dropName').textContent = u.profile.name;
document.getElementById('dropProgram').textContent = u.profile.program;
// Profile Card Details
const k = ['Usn','Adm','Roll','Exam','Dob','Phone','Email','Father','Mother','ParentPhone'];
const o = ['usn','adm','roll','examNum','dob','phone','email','father','mother','parentPhone'];
k.forEach((id, i) => document.getElementById('prof'+id).textContent = u.profile[o[i]]);
// Dashboard Math & Setup
document.getElementById('dashPctProg').textContent = u.academics.syllabusCovered;
document.getElementById('dashBarProg').style.width = u.academics.syllabusCovered;
document.getElementById('dashAssign').textContent = u.academics.assignments;
document.getElementById('dashIA').textContent = u.academics.internals;
// Dashboard - Attendance Logics
const att = u.academics.overallAtt;
document.getElementById('dashAtt').textContent = att + '%';
document.getElementById('dashAttBar').style.width = att + '%';
const attCard = document.getElementById('cardAttendance');
const attWarn = document.getElementById('attWarningBlock');
if(att < 75) {
attCard.classList.add('bg-red-light', 'border-red');
document.getElementById('dashAtt').classList.add('text-red');
document.getElementById('dashAttBar').style.background = '#ef4444';
attWarn.style.display = 'flex'; attWarn.style.color = '#ef4444'; attWarn.style.background = '#fecaca';
} else {
attCard.classList.remove('bg-red-light', 'border-red');
document.getElementById('dashAtt').classList.remove('text-red');
document.getElementById('dashAtt').classList.add('text-green');
document.getElementById('dashAttBar').style.background = '#22c55e';
attWarn.style.display = 'none';
}
// Dashboard - Finances
document.getElementById('dashTotalFees').textContent = u.finances.total;
document.getElementById('dashPaidFees').textContent = u.finances.paid;
document.getElementById('dashPendingFees').textContent = u.finances.pending;
document.getElementById('dashFeeDue').textContent = u.finances.due;
const btnStat = document.getElementById('dashFeeStatus');
btnStat.textContent = u.finances.status;
btnStat.className = 'status-badge ' + (u.finances.status === 'Cleared' ? 'completed' : 'unpaid');
// Populate Fee Page similarly
const fd = ['Total','Paid','Pend','Due'];
const fo = ['total','paid','pending','due'];
fd.forEach((id, i) => document.getElementById('feeDet'+id).textContent = u.finances[fo[i]]);
// Inbox & Notifications (Inject Top 3 into Notification Dropdown)
document.getElementById('notifBadgeCount').textContent = u.inbox.length;
document.getElementById('globalNotifList').innerHTML = u.inbox.map(ib => `
<div class="notif-item">
<div class="notif-icon bg-red-light text-red"><i data-lucide="mail" width="16"></i></div>
<div class="notif-content">
<h4>${ib.title}</h4>
<p>${ib.msg}</p>
<span>From: ${ib.from} • ${ib.date}</span>
</div>
</div>
`).join('');
document.getElementById('inboxContainer').innerHTML = u.inbox.map(ib => `
<div style="padding:1.5rem; border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0; display:flex; gap:1.5rem;">
<div style="width:40px; height:40px; border-radius:50%; background:#e0f2fe; color:#0284c7; display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:center;"><i data-lucide="mail"></i></div>
<div style="flex:1;">
<div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; margin-bottom:0.5rem;">
<strong style="color:#0f172a;">${ib.title}</strong>
<span style="font-size:0.8rem; color:#64748b;">${ib.date}</span>
</div>
<p style="color:#475569; margin:0 0 0.5rem 0; font-size:0.95rem;">${ib.msg}</p>
<span style="font-size:0.8rem; font-weight:600; color:#2A6F97;">- ${ib.from}</span>
</div>
</div>
`).join('');
// Full Timetable Mapping
const thr = `<tr><th>Time</th><th>Mon</th><th>Tue</th><th>Wed</th><th>Thu</th><th>Fri</th></tr>`;
const tbd = u.timetable.map(t => {
if(t.isBreak) return `<tr class="break-row"><td>${t.time}</td><td colspan="5">${t.name}</td></tr>`;
return `<tr><td><strong>${t.time}</strong></td><td>${t.m}</td><td>${t.t}</td><td>${t.w}</td><td>${t.th}</td><td>${t.f}</td></tr>`;
}).join('');
document.getElementById('timetableArea').innerHTML = thr + tbd;
// Dashboard Upcomings (Just slice first few classes)
document.getElementById('dashScheduleList').innerHTML = `
<div class="list-item-clean"><span>08:30 AM</span> <strong>${u.timetable[0].m}</strong></div>
<div class="list-item-clean"><span>09:30 AM</span> <strong>${u.timetable[1].m}</strong></div>
<div class="list-item-clean"><span>10:45 AM</span> <strong>${u.timetable[3].m}</strong></div>
`;
// Syllabus Matrix
document.getElementById('syllabusContentGrid').innerHTML = u.syllabus.map(s => `
<div class="erp-card">
<h3><i data-lucide="book-check"></i> ${s.sub}</h3>
<p style="font-size:0.85rem; color:#475569; border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9; padding-bottom:1rem;">${s.desc}</p>
<ul style="margin:1rem 0 0 0; padding-left:1.2rem; font-size:0.85rem; color:#1e293b; line-height:1.6;">
${s.mods.map(ch => `<li>${ch}</li>`).join('')}
</ul>
</div>
`).join('');
// Detailed Attendance Table
const ath = `<tr><th>Subject Code / Name</th><th>Attendance Percentage</th><th>Status Alert</th></tr>`;
const abd = u.attendance.map(a => {
const isBad = a.pct < 75;
const col = isBad ? '#ef4444' : '#22c55e';
const tag = isBad ? 'Shortage' : 'Satisfactory';
return `<tr>
<td><strong>${a.sub}</strong></td>
<td>
<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:1rem;">
<span style="font-weight:700; width:40px;">${a.pct}%</span>
<div class="progress-track" style="flex:1; margin:0;"><div class="progress-fill" style="width:${a.pct}%; background:${col};"></div></div>
</div>
</td>
<td><span class="status-badge" style="background:${isBad?'#fecaca':'#dcfce7'}; color:${col};">${tag}</span></td>
</tr>`;
}).join('');
document.getElementById('attendanceTable').innerHTML = ath + abd;
// Exams
// Generate full table
const renderEList = (exams) => {
const ehr = `<tr><th>Exam Type</th><th>Scheduled Date</th><th>Subject / Scope</th></tr>`;
const ebd = exams.map(e => `<tr><td><strong style="color:#0284c7;">${e.type}</strong></td><td>${e.date}</td><td>${e.sub}</td></tr>`).join('');
document.getElementById('examTable').innerHTML = ehr + ebd;
};
renderEList(u.exams);
// Wire the dropdown
document.getElementById('examFilterSelect').onchange = (e) => {
const val = e.target.value;
if(val === 'All') renderEList(u.exams);
else {
const filtered = u.exams.filter(ex => ex.type.includes(val) || val.includes(ex.type));
if(filtered.length === 0) document.getElementById('examTable').innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center; padding:2rem; color:#64748b;">No schedule posted for ${val}.</td></tr>`;
else renderEList(filtered);
}
};
// Assignments
document.getElementById('assignmentsContent').innerHTML = u.assignments.map(a => `
<div class="list-item-clean" style="padding:1rem 0;">
<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:1rem;">
<i data-lucide="${a.status === 'completed' ? 'check-circle-2' : 'circle-dashed'}" style="color: ${a.status === 'completed' ? '#22c55e' : '#eab308'}"></i>
<div>
<span style="font-weight:600; font-size:1rem; color:#1e293b; display:block;">${a.title}</span>
<span style="font-size:0.8rem; color:#64748b;">Due: ${a.date}</span>
</div>
</div>
<span class="status-badge ${a.status}">${a.status === 'completed' ? 'Submitted' : 'Pending Action'}</span>
</div>
`).join('');
// Staff Feedback
document.getElementById('feedbackCards').innerHTML = u.feedback.map(f => {
const stars = '★'.repeat(f.rating) + '☆'.repeat(5 - f.rating);
return `<div class="erp-card">
<div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; margin-bottom:1rem;">
<div>
<h4 style="margin:0; font-size:1.1rem; color:#0f172a;">${f.faculty}</h4>
<span style="font-size:0.8rem; color:#64748b;">${f.course}</span>
</div>
<div style="color:#eab308; font-size:1.2rem; letter-spacing:2px;">${stars}</div>
</div>
<p style="background:#f8fafc; padding:1rem; border-radius:6px; font-size:0.9rem; color:#475569; margin:0;">"${f.comment}"</p>
</div>`
}).join('');
}
async function hydrateStudentFromBackend() {
ry {
const [att, results, fees, complaints] = await Promise.all([
window.RRDCH_BACKEND.request("/student/attendance", { method: "GET" }),
window.RRDCH_BACKEND.request("/student/results?semester=4", { method: "GET" }),
window.RRDCH_BACKEND.request("/student/fees", { method: "GET" }),
window.RRDCH_BACKEND.request("/student/complaints", { method: "GET" })
]);
window.__studentFees = fees.data || [];
if ((att.data || []).length) {
const ath = `<tr><th>Subject Code / Name</th><th>Attendance Percentage</th><th>Status Alert</th></tr>`;
const abd = att.data.map(a => {
const pct = Number(a.percentage || 0);
const isBad = pct < 75;
const col = isBad ? '#ef4444' : '#22c55e';
const tag = isBad ? 'Shortage' : 'Satisfactory';
return `<tr>
<td><strong>${a.code || ''} - ${a.name || a.subject_name || 'Subject'}</strong></td>
<td><div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:1rem;"><span style="font-weight:700; width:40px;">${pct}%</span><div class="progress-track" style="flex:1; margin:0;"><div class="progress-fill" style="width:${pct}%; background:${col};"></div></div></div></td>
<td><span class="status-badge" style="background:${isBad?'#fecaca':'#dcfce7'}; color:${col};">${tag}</span></td>
</tr>`;
}).join('');
document.getElementById('attendanceTable').innerHTML = ath + abd;
}
if ((results.data || []).length) {
const ehr = `<tr><th>Exam Type</th><th>Scheduled Date</th><th>Subject / Scope</th></tr>`;
const ebd = results.data.map(r => `<tr><td><strong style="color:#0284c7;">Semester ${r.semester}</strong></td><td>${r.exam_date || "--"}</td><td>${r.subject_name || r.code || "Subject"} — ${r.marks_obtained || r.internal_marks || "--"} marks</td></tr>`).join('');
document.getElementById('examTable').innerHTML = ehr + ebd;
}
if ((fees.data || []).length) {
const pending = fees.data.filter(f => String(f.status || "").toLowerCase() !== "paid");
const totalDue = pending.reduce((sum, f) => sum + Number(f.amount || 0), 0);
if (totalDue > 0) {
document.getElementById('feePayInput').value = String(totalDue);
document.getElementById('dashPendingFees').textContent = "₹ " + totalDue.toLocaleString("en-IN");
}
}
if ((complaints.data || []).length) {
const list = complaints.data.map(c => `<div class="list-item-clean"><strong>${c.id}</strong><span style="color:#64748b;">${c.category} · ${c.status}</span></div>`).join('');
const host = document.getElementById('hostelComplaintsList');
if (host) host.innerHTML = list;
}
} catch (e) {
// Silent fallback to seeded local dataset.
}
}
// --- INTERACTIVE CALENDAR ENGINE ---
let currDate = new Date(); // Mock System considers "now"
function initCalendar() {
renderCal(currDate.getMonth(), currDate.getFullYear());
}
function renderCal(m, y) {
const calApp = document.getElementById('calendarApp');
const months = ["January", "February", "March", "April", "May", "June", "July", "August", "September", "October", "November", "December"];
// Events Global DB
const eventsDB = {
"0-26" : {type: "holiday", l: "Republic Day", i:"flag"},
"2-30" : {type: "holiday", l: "Good Friday", i:"flag"},
"3-13" : {type: "holiday", l: "Ugadi", i:"flag"},
"3-14" : {type: "holiday", l: "Ambedkar Jayanti", i:"flag"},
"3-18" : {type: "exam", l: "RGUHS Internal Assess", i:"file-edit"},
"3-22" : {type: "academic", l: "Mega Dental Camp", i:"stethoscope"},
"4-01" : {type: "holiday", l: "May Day", i:"flag"},
"4-20" : {type: "exam", l: "MDS Periodontology Internal", i:"file-edit"},
"5-05" : {type: "exam", l: "BDS Gen. Pathology Internal", i:"file-edit"},
"7-15" : {type: "holiday", l: "Independence Day", i:"flag"}
};
const firstDay = new Date(y, m, 1).getDay();
const daysInMonth = new Date(y, m + 1, 0).getDate();
const today = new Date();
let gridHTML = `<div class="cal-head">Sun</div><div class="cal-head">Mon</div><div class="cal-head">Tue</div><div class="cal-head">Wed</div><div class="cal-head">Thu</div><div class="cal-head">Fri</div><div class="cal-head">Sat</div>`;
for(let i = 0; i < firstDay; i++) {
gridHTML += `<div class="cal-day empty"></div>`;
}
for(let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
const isToday = (d === today.getDate() && m === today.getMonth() && y === today.getFullYear());
const eKey = `${m}-${d<10?'0'+d:d}`;
const ev = eventsDB[eKey];
let pillHTML = '';
if(ev) {
pillHTML = `<div class="event-pill event-${ev.type}"><i data-lucide="${ev.i}" width="10"></i> ${ev.l}</div>`;
}
gridHTML += `<div class="cal-day ${isToday ? 'today' : ''}" onclick="alert('Viewing events for ${d} ${months[m]} ${y}')">
<span class="cal-day-num" style="font-weight:${isToday?'700':'500'}">${d}</span>
${isToday && !ev ? `<div class="event-pill event-academic"><i data-lucide="play-circle" width="10"></i> Today</div>` : ''}
${pillHTML}
</div>`;
}
calApp.innerHTML = `
<div class="calendar-header">
<h3 style="margin: 0; font-size: 1.2rem;">${months[m]} ${y}</h3>
<div style="display:flex; gap:1rem;">
<button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding: 0.4rem 0.8rem;" onclick="chgMonth(-1)">&lt; Prev</button>
<button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding: 0.4rem 0.8rem;" onclick="currDate=new Date(); initCalendar();">Today Focus</button>
<button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding: 0.4rem 0.8rem;" onclick="chgMonth(1)">Next &gt;</button>
</div>
</div>
<div class="calendar-grid">
${gridHTML}
</div>
`;
lucide.createIcons();
}
window.chgMonth = (shift) => {
currDate.setMonth(currDate.getMonth() + shift);
initCalendar();
};
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
const target = document.querySelector('.split-text-target');
if(!target) return;
const lines = target.querySelectorAll('.split-line');
const charDelay = 30; // 30ms per character
const initialDelay = 200; // 200ms before starting
let prevLinesLength = 0;
lines.forEach((line) => {
const text = line.textContent.trim();
line.innerHTML = '';
line.style.display = 'block';
for(let charIndex = 0; charIndex < text.length; charIndex++) {
const char = text[charIndex];
const span = document.createElement('span');
span.textContent = char === ' ' ? '\u00A0' : char;
span.style.display = 'inline-block';
span.style.opacity = '0';
span.style.transform = 'translateX(-18px)';
span.style.transition = 'opacity 500ms ease-out, transform 500ms ease-out';
const delay = initialDelay + (prevLinesLength * charDelay) + (charIndex * charDelay);
span.style.transitionDelay = delay + 'ms';
line.appendChild(span);
// Trigger reflow & animate
requestAnimationFrame(() => {
setTimeout(() => {
span.style.opacity = '1';
span.style.transform = 'translateX(0)';
}, 50);
});
}
prevLinesLength += text.length;
});
});
</script>

<!-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════
ABOUT RRDCH
══════════════════════════════════════════════════ -->
<section id="about" class="container" style="padding-top:3rem;padding-bottom:4rem;">
<div class="grid-2" style="align-items:center;gap:4rem;">
<div class="animate-on-scroll">
<div class="section-tag">Est. 1992</div>
<h2 class="section-title" style="text-align:left;margin-top:0.5rem;margin-bottom:1rem;">About RRDCH</h2>
<p style="color:var(--cu-text-muted);margin-bottom:1rem;line-height:1.8;font-size:0.97rem;">
Established in 1992, Rajarajeshwari Dental College and Hospital has grown into a premier institution of dental education and research in India. Affiliated to Rajiv Gandhi University of Health Sciences (RGUHS) and recognized by the Dental Council of India (DCI).
</p>
<p style="color:var(--cu-text-muted);margin-bottom:1.75rem;line-height:1.8;font-size:0.97rem;">
Our mission is to foster comprehensive dental care, innovative research, and produce distinguished dental professionals who lead the field with integrity.
</p>
<ul style="list-style:none;display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:0.6rem;margin-bottom:2rem;">
<li style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.6rem;font-weight:600;font-size:0.92rem;">
<span style="width:20px;height:20px;background:var(--cu-gold-muted);border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:var(--cu-gold);font-size:0.75rem;flex-shrink:0;">✓</span>
Recognized by Dental Council of India (DCI)
</li>
<li style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.6rem;font-weight:600;font-size:0.92rem;">
<span style="width:20px;height:20px;background:var(--cu-gold-muted);border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:var(--cu-gold);font-size:0.75rem;flex-shrink:0;">✓</span>
Affiliated to RGUHS, Karnataka
</li>
<li style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.6rem;font-weight:600;font-size:0.92rem;">
<span style="width:20px;height:20px;background:var(--cu-gold-muted);border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:var(--cu-gold);font-size:0.75rem;flex-shrink:0;">✓</span>
ISO 9001:2015 Certified Institution
</li>
<li style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:0.6rem;font-weight:600;font-size:0.92rem;">
<span style="width:20px;height:20px;background:var(--cu-gold-muted);border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:var(--cu-gold);font-size:0.75rem;flex-shrink:0;">✓</span>
NABH Accredited Hospital
</li>

const contentArea = document.getElementById('degreeContent');
const searchInput = document.getElementById('degreeSearch');
const degreeSection = document.getElementById('degree-section');
let currentExpandedCourse = null;
// Fetch additional course details (local-only, no server needed)
async function fetchCourseDetails(courseId) {
return null; // Use local courseData only
}
function renderCourseDetail(course, backendData) {
const data = backendData?.data || course;
return `
<div class="course-detail-overlay" style="
position: fixed;
op: 0;
left: 0;
width: 100%;
height: 100%;
background: rgba(0,0,0,0.6);
backdrop-filter: blur(4px);
z-index: 1000;
display: flex;
align-items: center;
justify-content: center;
padding: 1rem;
animation: fadeIn 0.3s ease;
" onclick="if(event.target === this) closeCourseDetail()">
<div style="
background: white;
border-radius: 16px;
max-width: 600px;
width: 100%;
max-height: 90vh;
overflow-y: auto;
box-shadow: 0 25px 80px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
animation: slideUp 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1);
">
<div style="padding: 2rem;">
<div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start; margin-bottom: 1rem;">
<span style="font-size: 0.75rem; font-weight: 700; text-transform: uppercase; letter-spacing: 1px; color: var(--cu-gold); background: var(--cu-gold-muted); padding: 0.4rem 0.8rem; border-radius: 4px;">${course.dept}</span>
<button onclick="closeCourseDetail()" style="background: none; border: none; cursor: pointer; padding: 0.5rem; color: #64748b; hover: color: var(--cu-blue);">
<svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12"/></svg>
</button>
</div>
<h3 style="font-size: 1.5rem; font-weight: 800; color: var(--cu-blue); margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">${course.name}</h3>
<div style="display: flex; gap: 1rem; margin-bottom: 1.5rem; flex-wrap: wrap;">
<span style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: #64748b; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 0.3rem;">
<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><polyline points="12 6 12 12 16 14"/></svg>
${course.dur}
</span>
<span style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: #64748b; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 0.3rem;">
<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M17 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-4-4H5a4 4 0 0 0-4 4v2"/><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="4"/><path d="M23 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-3-3.87"/></svg>
${course.seats} Seats
</span>
<span style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: var(--cu-blue); font-weight: 700; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 0.3rem;">
<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M12 1v22M17 5H9.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 0 0 7h5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 0 7H6"/></svg>
${course.fees}
</span>
</div>
<p style="color: #475569; line-height: 1.7; margin-bottom: 1.5rem;">${course.desc}</p>
<div style="display: flex; gap: 1rem;">
<a href="admission_enquiry.html?course=${encodeURIComponent(course.id)}" style="flex: 1; background: var(--cu-blue); color: white; text-align: center; padding: 0.875rem; border-radius: 8px; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; transition: all 0.2s;">Apply Now</a>
<a href="departments.html?dept=${encodeURIComponent(course.dept)}" style="flex: 1; background: var(--cu-bg); color: var(--cu-blue); text-align: center; padding: 0.875rem; border-radius: 8px; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; border: 2px solid var(--cu-border); transition: all 0.2s;">View Department</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
`;
}
window.closeCourseDetail = function() {
const overlay = document.querySelector('.course-detail-overlay');
if (overlay) {
overlay.style.animation = 'fadeOut 0.2s ease forwards';
setTimeout(() => overlay.remove(), 200);
}
currentExpandedCourse = null;
};
async function showCourseDetail(course) {
if (currentExpandedCourse === course.id) {
closeCourseDetail();
return;
}
currentExpandedCourse = course.id;
closeCourseDetail(); // Close any existing
const backendData = await fetchCourseDetails(course.id);
const detailHTML = renderCourseDetail(course, backendData);
document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', detailHTML);
}
function renderCourses(term, tabName) {
if(!contentArea) return;
const courses = tabName ? courseData[tabName] : Object.values(courseData).flat();
const filtered = courses.filter(c => c.name.toLowerCase().includes((term || '').toLowerCase()));
if(filtered.length === 0) {
contentArea.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--cu-text-muted); padding:1rem 0;">No matching courses found.</div>';
return;
}
contentArea.innerHTML = filtered.map((c, i) => `
<div class="course-card" data-course-id="${c.id}" style="
background: white;
border: 2px solid var(--cu-border);
padding: 1.25rem;
border-radius: 12px;
margin-bottom: 0.75rem;
display: flex;
justify-content: space-between;
align-items: center;
box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.04);
cursor: pointer;
ransition: all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1);
animation: fadeUp 0.4s ease backwards;
animation-delay: ${i * 0.05}s;
" onmouseenter="this.style.borderColor='var(--cu-gold)'; this.style.transform='translateY(-3px) scale(1.01)'; this.style.boxShadow='0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)'" onmouseleave="this.style.borderColor='var(--cu-border)'; this.style.transform=''; this.style.boxShadow='0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'">
<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 1rem; flex: 1;">
<div style="width: 48px; height: 48px; border-radius: 10px; background: linear-gradient(135deg, var(--cu-blue), var(--cu-blue-light)); display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; color: white; font-weight: 700; font-size: 0.875rem;">
${c.id.split('-')[0].toUpperCase()}
</div>
<div>
<div style="font-weight: 700; color: var(--cu-blue); font-size: 1rem; margin-bottom: 0.25rem;">${c.name}</div>
<div style="font-size: 0.8rem; color: #64748b;">${c.dept} • ${c.seats} seats</div>
</div>
</div>
<span style="font-size: 0.8rem; color: #64748b; font-weight: 600; background: var(--cu-bg); padding: 0.4rem 0.9rem; border-radius: 20px;">${c.dur}</span>
</div>
`).join('');
// Add click handlers
contentArea.querySelectorAll('.course-card').forEach((card, idx) => {
card.addEventListener('click', () => showCourseDetail(filtered[idx]));
});
}
// Tab click handlers
document.querySelectorAll('.degree-tab').forEach(tab => {
ab.addEventListener('click', () => {
document.querySelectorAll('.degree-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
ab.classList.add('active');
searchInput.value = '';
renderCourses('', tab.innerText.trim());
});
});
if (searchInput) {
searchInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
document.querySelectorAll('.degree-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
renderCourses(e.target.value, null);
});
}
// Search button click handler
const searchBtn = document.getElementById('degreeSearchBtn');
if (searchBtn) {
searchBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
const query = searchInput.value.trim();
if (query) {
document.querySelectorAll('.degree-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
renderCourses(query, null);
}
});
}
// Scroll-based hide/show for degree section
if (degreeSection) {
let lastScrollY = 0;
let sectionTop = degreeSection.offsetTop;
let sectionHeight = degreeSection.offsetHeight;
const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
entries.forEach(entry => {
if (entry.isIntersecting) {
degreeSection.style.opacity = '1';
degreeSection.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
degreeSection.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
}
});
}, { threshold: 0.1 });
observer.observe(degreeSection);
// Hide when scrolled past
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
const scrollY = window.scrollY;
const sectionBottom = sectionTop + sectionHeight;
// Hide when scrolled well past the section
if (scrollY > sectionBottom + 100) {
degreeSection.style.opacity = '0';
degreeSection.style.transform = 'translateY(-20px)';
degreeSection.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
degreeSection.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease, transform 0.5s ease';
} else if (scrollY < sectionBottom) {
degreeSection.style.opacity = '1';
degreeSection.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
degreeSection.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
}
lastScrollY = scrollY;
}, { passive: true });
// Update on resize
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
sectionTop = degreeSection.offsetTop;
sectionHeight = degreeSection.offsetHeight;
});
}
// Init default
renderCourses('', 'UNDERGRADUATE (BDS)');
})();
// Review rating
let fbRating = 0;
function setRating(n) {
fbRating = n;
document.querySelectorAll('.fstar').forEach((s, i) => {
s.style.color = i < n ? '#f59e0b' : '#cbd5e1';
});
}
function submitFeedback() {
const name = document.getElementById('fbName').value.trim();
const msg = document.getElementById('fbMsg').value.trim();
if (!name || !msg || fbRating === 0) {
alert('Please fill in your name, select a star rating, and write a review.');
return;
}
document.getElementById('fbSuccess').style.display = 'block';
document.getElementById('fbName').value = '';
document.getElementById('fbRole').value = '';
document.getElementById('fbMsg').value = '';
fbRating = 0;
document.querySelectorAll('.fstar').forEach(s => s.style.color = '#cbd5e1');
setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('fbSuccess').style.display = 'none', 4000);
}
// Degree tab switching function
function showDegree(degree) {
// Hide all content
document.querySelectorAll('.degree-content').forEach(content => {
content.style.display = 'none';
});
// Show selected content
document.getElementById(degree + '-content').style.display = 'block';
// Update active tab
document.querySelectorAll('.degree-tab').forEach(tab => {
ab.classList.remove('active');
});
document.querySelector('[data-degree="' + degree + '"]').classList.add('active');
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

Founded in 1992 under the Rajiv Gandhi Group of Institutions and the Moogambigai Charitable and Educational Trust, RRDCH was established with a vision to provide exceptional dental education and community-focused healthcare. Beginning with only 40 admissions in the Bachelor of Dental Surgery (BDS) program, the college has undergone exponential growth over three decades.
</p>
<p style="font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'SF Pro Text', sans-serif; font-size: 0.95rem; letter-spacing: -0.01em; color: var(--text-muted); line-height: 1.7; text-align: center;">
Today, the campus houses over 250 modern dental units and chairs, with a comprehensive General Hospital treating 450-500 patients daily. Our 12 specialized OPD clinics provide postgraduate dental students with extensive clinical training.
</p>

<script>
(function(){
const form = document.getElementById('contactForm');
if (!form) return;
form.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
e.preventDefault();
const name = document.getElementById('contactName')?.value.trim();
const email = document.getElementById('contactEmail')?.value.trim();
const subject = document.getElementById('subject')?.value.trim();
const message = document.getElementById('message')?.value.trim();
if (!name || !email || !subject || !message) return;
const btn = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
const prev = btn.textContent;
btn.disabled = true;
btn.textContent = 'Sending...';
ry {
const res = await fetch('/api/contact', {
method: 'POST',
headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
body: JSON.stringify({ name, email, subject, message })
});
const data = await res.json();
if (!res.ok || data.ok === false) throw new Error(data.msg || 'Failed');
document.getElementById('contactSuccess').style.display = 'block';
form.reset();
setTimeout(() => { document.getElementById('contactSuccess').style.display = 'none'; }, 4500);
} catch (err) {
window.RRDCH_UTILS?.showToast(err.message || 'Could not send message.', 'error');
} finally {
btn.disabled = false;
btn.textContent = prev;
}
});
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
========== ./js/gallery-dynamic.js ==========
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
const galleryContainer = document.getElementById('dynamic-masonry-container');
if (!galleryContainer) return;
if (typeof ALL_GALLERY_IMAGES === 'undefined' || !ALL_GALLERY_IMAGES.length) {
galleryContainer.innerHTML = '<p>No images found.</p>';
return;
}
// Filter out logos just in case
const validImages = ALL_GALLERY_IMAGES.filter(src => !src.includes('/logos/'));
// Shuffle array (Fisher-Yates)
for (let i = validImages.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
[validImages[i], validImages[j]] = [validImages[j], validImages[i]];
}
// We will build 4 tracks. Let's use up to 160 images total (40 per track) to keep DOM healthy but look infinite
const numTracks = 4;
const imagesPerTrack = 40;
const tracks = [[], [], [], []];
let imgIndex = 0;
for (let i = 0; i < numTracks; i++) {
for (let j = 0; j < imagesPerTrack; j++) {
if (imgIndex >= validImages.length) {
imgIndex = 0; // Wrap around if we run out (unlikely with 600)
}
racks[i].push(validImages[imgIndex]);
imgIndex++;
}
}
const columnSpeeds = ['col-down', 'col-up', 'col-down-slow', 'col-up-fast'];
const trackClasses = ['track-1', 'track-2', 'track-3', 'track-4'];
const shapeClasses = ['tall', 'wide', 'square'];
let html = '';
racks.forEach((trackImages, colIndex) => {
html += `<div class="masonry-column ${columnSpeeds[colIndex]}">`;
html += `<div class="masonry-track ${trackClasses[colIndex]}" id="galleryTrack${colIndex}">`;
rackImages.forEach((src) => {
// Assign random shape to give the masonry look
const randomShape = shapeClasses[Math.floor(Math.random() * shapeClasses.length)];
html += `
<div class="masonry-item ${randomShape}">
<img src="${src}" alt="Campus Experience" loading="lazy">
</div>
`;
});
// Duplicate the first few images to make the CSS infinite scroll loop seamlessly
for(let j=0; j<8; j++) {
const randomShape = shapeClasses[Math.floor(Math.random() * shapeClasses.length)];
html += `
<div class="masonry-item ${randomShape}">
<img src="${trackImages[j]}" alt="Campus Experience" loading="lazy">
</div>
`;
}
html += `</div></div>`;
});
galleryContainer.innerHTML = html;
});
// Pause/Play functionality
window.toggleGalleryAnimation = function(state) {
for (let i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
const track = document.getElementById('galleryTrack' + i);
if (track) {
rack.style.animationPlayState = state;
}
}
};
========== ./js/ai.js ==========
// ai.js — RRDCH AI chatbot using Gemini REST API directly (no server needed)
(function initRRDCHAi() {
const GEMINI_KEY = 'AIzaSyBhCpDnWo8u_GdHfu7ermBLbnABuOJVA4U';
const GEMINI_URL = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent?key=${GEMINI_KEY}`;
function isConfigured() { return true; }
async function callGemini(promptText) {
ry {
const res = await fetch(GEMINI_URL, {
method: 'POST',
headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: promptText }] }] })
});
const data = await res.json();
const text = data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
if (!text) throw new Error('Empty response from Gemini');
return text;
} catch (e) {
console.warn('[RRDCH AI] Gemini API error:', e);
hrow new Error('AI request failed. Please try again.');
}
}
async function askText(systemPrompt, history) {
const last = history?.[history.length - 1]?.parts?.[0]?.text || '';
const ctx = window.RRDCH_SITE_CONTEXT ? window.RRDCH_SITE_CONTEXT.join ? window.RRDCH_SITE_CONTEXT.join('\n') : String(window.RRDCH_SITE_CONTEXT) : '';
const merged = `${systemPrompt}\n\nInstitutional context (RRDCH Bangalore — use for factual answers):\n${ctx}\n\nUser question: ${last}`;
const text = await callGemini(merged);
// Log to Supabase if available
if (window.sb) {
ry { await window.sb.from('chatbot_sessions').insert({ query: last, response: text, mode: 'site-assistant', urgency: 'Routine', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch (_) {}
}
return text.trim();
}
async function askJson(promptText) {
const sysPrompt = `You are a dental triage assistant for RRDCH Bangalore. Analyze the patient's symptoms and respond ONLY with a JSON object in this exact format:
{
"urgency": "Routine" | "Soon" | "Urgent" | "Emergency",
"department": "Department Name",
"advice": "Brief patient-friendly advice",
"selfCare": ["tip1", "tip2"]
}
Patient symptoms: ${promptText}`;
const text = await callGemini(sysPrompt);
// Extract JSON from response
const match = text.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
if (match) {
ry {
const parsed = JSON.parse(match[0]);
// Log to Supabase
if (window.sb) {
ry { await window.sb.from('chatbot_sessions').insert({ query: promptText, mode: 'symptom-checker', urgency: parsed.urgency || 'Routine', department: parsed.department || '', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch (_) {}
}
return parsed;
} catch (_) {}
}
return { urgency: 'Routine', department: 'General Dentistry', advice: text, selfCare: [] };
}
window.RRDCH_AI = {
isConfigured,
askText,
askJson,
callGemini,
};
})();

// public-shell.js — RRDCH Shared Header + Drawer + Footer
(function initPublicShell() {
const LANG_KEY = "rrdch_lang";
function getLang() {
return (localStorage.getItem(LANG_KEY) || "").trim() === "kn" ? "kn" : "en";
}
function setLang(lang) {
const next = lang === "kn" ? "kn" : "en";
localStorage.setItem(LANG_KEY, next);
document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-lang", next);
document.documentElement.setAttribute("lang", next);
return next;
}
function removeIfExists(selector) {
document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach((n) => n.remove());
}
function markCurrentPath(root) {
const currentPath = window.location.pathname.split("/").pop() || "index.html";
root.querySelectorAll("a[href]").forEach((link) => {
const lp = (link.getAttribute("href") || "").split("#")[0];
if (lp && lp === currentPath) link.classList.add("active");
});
}
function renderShell({ pageId }) {
// Clean up lang
const lang = getLang();
document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-lang", lang);
document.documentElement.setAttribute("lang", lang);
document.body.classList.add("public-page", "public-shell-mounted");
if (pageId) document.body.classList.add(`page-${pageId.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/gi, "-").toLowerCase()}`);
// Remove any previous shells
removeIfExists("#rrdch-public-shell");
removeIfExists("footer.footer");
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
//  GLOBAL LANGUAGE FUNCTIONS (must be before shell creation)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
window.RRDCH_LANG = {
get: function() {
return localStorage.getItem('rrdch_lang') || 'en';
},
set: function(lang) {
localStorage.setItem('rrdch_lang', lang);
document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-lang', lang);
document.documentElement.setAttribute('lang', lang);
// Dispatch custom event for other components
window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('rrdch:langchange', { detail: { lang } }));
},
oggle: function() {
const current = this.get();
const next = current === 'en' ? 'kn' : 'en';
his.set(next);
return next;
}
};
