const backdrop     = shell.querySelector("#drawerBackdrop");
const closeBtn     = shell.querySelector("#drawerCloseBtn");
const drawerLeft   = shell.querySelector("#drawerLeft");
const drawerRight  = shell.querySelector("#drawerRight");
function openDrawer() {
document.body.classList.add("nav-drawer-open");
drawer.setAttribute("aria-hidden", "false");
menuBtn.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
// Focus trap — focus first link inside drawer
setTimeout(() => {
drawerRight.querySelector("a, button")?.focus();
}, 420);
}
function closeDrawer() {
document.body.classList.remove("nav-drawer-open");
drawer.setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
menuBtn.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
menuBtn.focus();
}
menuBtn?.addEventListener("click", () => {
if (document.body.classList.contains("nav-drawer-open")) closeDrawer();
else openDrawer();
});
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
//  LANGUAGE TOGGLE WIRING (shell-level)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
const langBtn = shell.querySelector("#langToggle");
if (langBtn) {
// Helper to update UI
function updateLangUI(lang) {
const spanEn = langBtn.querySelector("#lang-en");
const spanKn = langBtn.querySelector("#lang-kn");
if (spanEn) { 
spanEn.classList.toggle("active", lang === "en"); 
spanEn.style.opacity = lang === "en" ? "1" : "0.5"; 
}
if (spanKn) { 
spanKn.classList.toggle("active", lang === "kn"); 
spanKn.style.opacity = lang === "kn" ? "1" : "0.5"; 
}
// Also sync any other elements with these IDs
document.querySelectorAll("#lang-en").forEach(el => {
el.classList.toggle("active", lang === "en");
});
document.querySelectorAll("#lang-kn").forEach(el => {
el.classList.toggle("active", lang === "kn");
});
// Trigger translation
if (window.RRDCH_I18N && typeof window.RRDCH_I18N.apply === 'function') {
window.RRDCH_I18N.apply();
}
}
// Sync initial state
const _curLang = window.RRDCH_LANG ? window.RRDCH_LANG.get() : (localStorage.getItem('rrdch_lang') || 'en');
updateLangUI(_curLang);
// Handle click
langBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
const next = window.RRDCH_LANG ? window.RRDCH_LANG.toggle() : (() => {
const current = localStorage.getItem('rrdch_lang') || 'en';
const next = current === 'en' ? 'kn' : 'en';
localStorage.setItem('rrdch_lang', next);
document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-lang', next);
document.documentElement.setAttribute('lang', next);
return next;
})();
updateLangUI(next);
});
// Listen for language change events from other components
window.addEventListener('rrdch:langchange', (e) => {
updateLangUI(e.detail.lang);
});
}
closeBtn?.addEventListener("click", closeDrawer);
backdrop?.addEventListener("click", closeDrawer);
// Accordion Logic for Nested Menus
const accordions = drawer.querySelectorAll(".cu-accordion.has-submenu");
accordions.forEach(acc => {
const btn = acc.querySelector(".cu-accordion-btn");
const content = acc.querySelector(".cu-accordion-content");
if (btn && content) {
btn.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
e.preventDefault();
const isOpen = acc.classList.contains("active");
// Close others to keep UI clean
accordions.forEach(other => {
if (other !== acc) {
other.classList.remove("active");
const otherContent = other.querySelector(".cu-accordion-content");
if (otherContent) otherContent.style.maxHeight = null;
}
});
// Toggle current
if (isOpen) {
acc.classList.remove("active");
content.style.maxHeight = null;
} else {
acc.classList.add("active");
content.style.maxHeight = content.scrollHeight + "px";
}
});
}
});
// Close on any terminal link click inside drawer
drawer.querySelectorAll("a[href]").forEach((link) => {
if (!link.classList.contains("cu-accordion-btn")) {
link.addEventListener("click", () => setTimeout(closeDrawer, 80));
}
});
// Keyboard: Escape
document.addEventListener("keydown", (e) => {
if (e.key === "Escape" && document.body.classList.contains("nav-drawer-open")) {
closeDrawer();
}
});
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
//  SCROLL FX — add scrolled class for glass effect
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
const header = shell.querySelector("#siteHeader");
let scrollTicking = false;
window.addEventListener("scroll", () => {
if (scrollTicking) return;
scrollTicking = true;
requestAnimationFrame(() => {
const y = window.scrollY || 0;
if (header) {
if (y > 50) {
header.classList.add("scrolled");
} else {
header.classList.remove("scrolled");
}
}
scrollTicking = false;
});
}, { passive: true });
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
//  RE-INIT LUCIDE icons for dynamically created shell
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
if (window.lucide) {
window.lucide.createIcons();
} else {
window.addEventListener("load", () => {
if (window.lucide) window.lucide.createIcons();
});
}
// ─── Expose API ───
window.RRDCH_PUBLIC_SHELL = window.RRDCH_PUBLIC_SHELL || {};
window.RRDCH_PUBLIC_SHELL.pageId      = pageId || "";
window.RRDCH_PUBLIC_SHELL.openDrawer  = openDrawer;
window.RRDCH_PUBLIC_SHELL.closeDrawer = closeDrawer;
// Backend: Supabase-only, no local server needed

// backend.js — RRDCH Supabase-direct connector (no Node server required)
(function initRRDCHBackend() {
const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://hbalflsjvtovtmmypdvv.supabase.co';
const SUPABASE_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6ImhiYWxmbHNqdnRvdnRtbXlwZHZ2Iiwicm9sZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzY1MDc1OTcsImV4cCI6MjA5MjA4MzU5N30.iq60dhhWA8oqwNHQr6R4hvnCDKNBZ-sP-1A2PXxkkRU';
const TOKEN_KEY = 'rrdch_token';
const DOCTOR_SESSION_KEY = 'rrdch_doctor_session';
// No localhost server. API_BASE kept for backwards compat but unused.
const API_BASE = SUPABASE_URL;
function getToken() { return localStorage.getItem(TOKEN_KEY) || ''; }
function setToken(token) { if (token) localStorage.setItem(TOKEN_KEY, token); }
function getDoctorSession() { return localStorage.getItem(DOCTOR_SESSION_KEY) || ''; }
function setDoctorSession(token) { if (token) localStorage.setItem(DOCTOR_SESSION_KEY, token); }
// Generic Supabase REST helper
async function supabaseRequest(table, options = {}) {
const method = options.method || 'GET';
const url = `${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/${table}${options.query || ''}`;
const headers = {
'apikey': SUPABASE_KEY,
'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPABASE_KEY,
'Content-Type': 'application/json',
'Prefer': options.prefer || 'return=representation'
};
ry {
const res = await fetch(url, { method, headers, body: options.body });
if (!res.ok) return { ok: false, data: null };
const data = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
return { ok: true, data };
} catch (e) {
console.warn('[RRDCH] Supabase request failed:', e);
return { ok: false, data: null };
}
}
// Backwards-compat request stub (won't 404 — just returns fallback)
async function request(path, options = {}) {
console.warn('[RRDCH] backend.request() called for', path, '— using Supabase directly instead.');
return { ok: true, data: [] };
}
// Doctor login via Supabase
async function doctorLogin(email, password) {
if (window.sb) {
ry {
const { data, error } = await window.sb.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
if (!error && data.user) {
setDoctorSession(data.session?.access_token || 'demo-token');
return { ok: true, data: { token: data.session?.access_token } };
}
} catch (e) {}
}
// Demo fallback
if (email === 'doctor@rrdch.in' && password === 'doctor123') {
setDoctorSession('demo-token');
return { ok: true, data: { token: 'demo-token' } };
}
hrow new Error('Invalid credentials.');
}
// No-op track (was calling /api/track)
async function trackVisit(payload) {
if (window.sb) {
ry { await window.sb.from('admin_audit_log').insert({ action: 'page_visit', ...payload }); } catch (_) {}
}
return { ok: true };
}
// Doctor request (was calling /api/doctor/:path)
async function doctorRequest(path, options = {}) {
// Route to Supabase equivalents
if (path === 'login') return doctorLogin(options._email, options._password);
return { ok: true, data: [] };
}
function normalizeDeptName(name) {
const key = (name || '').toLowerCase();
if (key.includes('oral surgery')) return 'Oral & Maxillofacial Surgery';
if (key.includes('orthodontics')) return 'Orthodontics & Dentofacial Orthopedics';
if (key.includes('periodontology')) return 'Periodontology';
if (key.includes('conservative')) return 'Conservative Dentistry & Endodontics';
if (key.includes('general')) return 'Public Health Dentistry';
return name || '';
}
let cachedDepartments = null;
async function getDepartments() {
if (cachedDepartments) return cachedDepartments;
// Try Supabase first
const res = await supabaseRequest('opd_queue', { query: '?select=department', method: 'GET' });
if (res.ok && res.data && res.data.length > 0) {
cachedDepartments = [...new Set(res.data.map(r => r.department).filter(Boolean))].map((n, i) => ({ id: i + 1, name: n }));
} else {
cachedDepartments = [
{ id: 1, name: 'Oral Surgery' },
{ id: 2, name: 'Orthodontics' },
{ id: 3, name: 'General Dentistry' },
{ id: 4, name: 'Periodontology' },
{ id: 5, name: 'Conservative Dentistry & Endodontics' },
{ id: 6, name: 'Pedodontics' },
{ id: 7, name: 'Implantology' }
];
}
return cachedDepartments;
}
async function getDeptIdByName(name) {
const departments = await getDepartments();
const normalized = normalizeDeptName(name);
const match = departments.find(function(d) {
const n = (d.name || '').toLowerCase();
return n.includes(normalized.toLowerCase()) || normalized.toLowerCase().includes(n);
});
return match ? match.id : null;
}
window.RRDCH_BACKEND = {
API_BASE,
SUPABASE_URL,
SUPABASE_KEY,
request,
supabaseRequest,
getToken,
setToken,
getDoctorSession,
setDoctorSession,
getDepartments,
getDeptIdByName,
doctorRequest,
doctorLogin,
rackVisit,
};
})();

// ════════ NAVIGATION ════════
function initActiveNav() {
const currentPath = window.location.pathname.split('/').pop() || 'index.html';
document.querySelectorAll('.nav-links .nav-link, [data-nav-link]').forEach(link => {
const linkPath = link.getAttribute('href')?.split('#')[0];
if (linkPath === currentPath && linkPath !== '') link.classList.add('active');
});
}
function initPopupNav() {
document.querySelectorAll('.has-popup').forEach(toggle => {
oggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
e.preventDefault();
const parent = toggle.parentElement;
document.querySelectorAll('.popup-nav-item.open').forEach(item => {
if (item !== parent) item.classList.remove('open');
});
parent.classList.toggle('open');
});
});
document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
if (!e.target.closest('.popup-nav-item')) {
document.querySelectorAll('.popup-nav-item.open').forEach(item => item.classList.remove('open'));
}
});
}
// ════════ CAROUSEL ════════
function initCarousel() {
const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.slide');
const dots = document.querySelectorAll('.dot');
if(slides.length === 0) return;
let currentSlide = 0;
function goToSlide(n) {
slides[currentSlide].classList.remove('active');
dots[currentSlide]?.classList.remove('active');
currentSlide = (n + slides.length) % slides.length;
slides[currentSlide].classList.add('active');
dots[currentSlide]?.classList.add('active');
}
dots.forEach((dot, index) => dot.addEventListener('click', () => goToSlide(index)));
setInterval(() => goToSlide(currentSlide + 1), 4000);
}
// ════════ SCROLL ANIMATIONS ════════
function initAnimations() {
const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
entries.forEach(entry => { 
if(entry.isIntersecting) {
entry.target.classList.add('is-visible'); 
observer.unobserve(entry.target); // Run once
}
});
}, { threshold: 0.15, rootMargin: "0px 0px -50px 0px" });
document.querySelectorAll('.animate-on-scroll').forEach(el => observer.observe(el));
}
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
initAnimations();
});
// ════════ LANGUAGE ════════
function initLanguageToggle() {
const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('langToggle');
if(!toggleBtn) return;
// restore persisted language if present
const persisted = localStorage.getItem("rrdch_lang");
if (persisted === "kn" || persisted === "en") currentLang = persisted;
document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-lang", currentLang);
document.documentElement.setAttribute("lang", currentLang);
document.getElementById('lang-en')?.classList.toggle('active', currentLang === 'en');
document.getElementById('lang-kn')?.classList.toggle('active', currentLang === 'kn');
oggleBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
currentLang = currentLang === 'en' ? 'kn' : 'en';
localStorage.setItem("rrdch_lang", currentLang);
document.documentElement.setAttribute("data-lang", currentLang);
document.documentElement.setAttribute("lang", currentLang);
document.getElementById('lang-en')?.classList.toggle('active', currentLang === 'en');
document.getElementById('lang-kn')?.classList.toggle('active', currentLang === 'kn');
window.RRDCH_I18N?.apply();
});
}
// Lightweight DOM i18n applier (public pages + any page using data-i18n)
window.RRDCH_I18N = {
apply: function(root = document) {
const lang = (localStorage.getItem("rrdch_lang") === "kn") ? "kn" : "en";
currentLang = lang;
root.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n]').forEach(el => {
const key = el.getAttribute('data-i18n');
const val = translations[lang] && translations[lang][key] ? translations[lang][key] : "";
if (!val) return;
// Allow HTML for a small set (addresses, copyright)
if (key.startsWith("footer_") || key.startsWith("ticker_") || key === "site_title" || key === "footer_address") {
el.innerHTML = val;
} else {
el.textContent = val.replace(/&amp;/g, "&");
}
});
}
};
// ════════ FORMS ════════
function initForms() {
document.querySelectorAll('form[data-validate="true"]').forEach(form => {
form.addEventListener('submit', (e) => {
e.preventDefault();
let isValid = true;
form.querySelectorAll('[required]').forEach(input => {
if(!input.value.trim()) { input.classList.add('is-invalid'); isValid = false; }
else input.classList.remove('is-invalid');
});
if(isValid) {
const btn = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
const origText = btn.innerHTML;
btn.innerHTML = 'Processing...'; btn.disabled = true;
setTimeout(() => {
form.style.display = 'none';
const successDiv = document.createElement('div');
successDiv.className = 'success-message';
if (form.id === 'bookingForm') {
const dr = form.querySelector('#doctor')?.value;
const date = form.querySelector('#date')?.value;
successDiv.innerHTML = `
<div class="success-icon"><i class="lucide-check">✓</i></div>
<h3>Booking Confirmed!</h3>
<p>Your appointment has been successfully scheduled.</p>
<div class="appointment-ticket">
<div class="ticket-row"><span>Token No:</span> <strong>#RRD-402</strong></div>
<div class="ticket-row"><span>Doctor:</span> <strong>${dr || 'Assigned Dr'}</strong></div>
<div class="ticket-row"><span>Date:</span> <strong>${date || 'Today'}</strong></div>
<div class="ticket-row"><span>Est. Time:</span> <strong>10:30 AM</strong></div>
</div>
<button class="btn btn-primary" style="margin-top: 1rem" onclick="location.reload()">Done</button>`;
} else {
successDiv.innerHTML = `
<div class="success-icon"><i class="lucide-check">✓</i></div>
<h3>Submitted Successfully!</h3>
<p>Your request has been recorded.</p>
<button class="btn btn-outline" style="margin-top: 1rem" onclick="location.reload()">Done</button>`;
}
form.parentNode.appendChild(successDiv);
}, 1500);
}
});
form.querySelectorAll('.form-control').forEach(input => {
input.addEventListener('input', () => input.classList.remove('is-invalid'));
});
});
}
// ════════ QUEUE SYSTEM (fallback) ════════
function initQueueSystem() {
const queueElement = document.getElementById('dynamicQueue');
if(queueElement) {
let queuePos = 3;
setInterval(() => {
if(Math.random() > 0.8 && queuePos > 0) {
queuePos--;
queueElement.innerHTML = queuePos === 0 ? "It's your turn!" : `You are <strong>#${queuePos}</strong> in line.`;
queueElement.parentElement.classList.add('pulse');
setTimeout(() => queueElement.parentElement.classList.remove('pulse'), 2000);
}
}, 5000);
}
}
// ════════ ANIMATED STATS ════════
function initAnimatedStats() {
const sections = document.querySelectorAll('.stats-section');
if (sections.length === 0) return;
const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
entries.forEach(entry => {
if (entry.isIntersecting) {
entry.target.querySelectorAll('.stat-number').forEach(el => {
const target = +el.getAttribute('data-target');
const duration = 2000; // 2 seconds
let startTimestamp = null;
const easeOutQuad = (t) => t * (2 - t);
const step = (timestamp) => {
if (!startTimestamp) startTimestamp = timestamp;
const progress = Math.min((timestamp - startTimestamp) / duration, 1);
el.innerText = Math.floor(easeOutQuad(progress) * target);
if (progress < 1) {
requestAnimationFrame(step);
} else {
el.innerText = target;
}
};
requestAnimationFrame(step);
});
observer.unobserve(entry.target);
}
});
}, { threshold: 0.5, rootMargin: "0px 0px -50px 0px" });
sections.forEach(sec => observer.observe(sec));
}
// ════════ DEPARTMENT SEARCH ════════
function initDeptSearch() {
const searchInput = document.getElementById('deptSearch');
if(!searchInput) return;
const cards = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.dept-card'));
const noResults = document.getElementById('deptNoResults');
const tagWrap = document.getElementById('deptTagFilters');
let activeTag = 'all';
function applyFilters() {
const term = (searchInput.value || '').toLowerCase().trim();
let visibleCount = 0;
cards.forEach(card => {
const text = (card.innerText + ' ' + (card.dataset.tags || '') + ' ' + (card.dataset.keywords || '')).toLowerCase();
const tags = (card.dataset.tags || '').toLowerCase().split(/\s+/);
const matchesSearch = !term || text.includes(term);
const matchesTag = activeTag === 'all' || tags.includes(activeTag);
const show = matchesSearch && matchesTag;
card.style.display = show ? '' : 'none';
card.style.boxShadow = show ? '0 0 0 1px rgba(42,111,151,0.18)' : '';
if (show) visibleCount++;
});
if (noResults) noResults.style.display = visibleCount === 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
}
searchInput.addEventListener('input', applyFilters);
if (tagWrap) {
agWrap.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
const btn = e.target.closest('[data-tag]');
if (!btn) return;
activeTag = btn.dataset.tag || 'all';
agWrap.querySelectorAll('[data-tag]').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
btn.classList.add('active');
applyFilters();
});
}
applyFilters();
}
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  ACCESSIBILITY TOOLBAR (injected dynamically)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════
function injectAccessibilityToolbar() {
/* Top accessibility strip removed per UX — keep API for any legacy onclick handlers. */
}
window._a11yFontSize = 100;
window.a11yFontChange = function(delta) {
window._a11yFontSize = Math.max(80, Math.min(140, window._a11yFontSize + delta));
document.documentElement.style.fontSize = window._a11yFontSize + "%";
localStorage.setItem("a11y_font", window._a11yFontSize);
};
window.a11yToggle = function(className, btnId) {
document.body.classList.toggle(className);
const on = document.body.classList.contains(className);
localStorage.setItem("a11y_" + className, on);
document.getElementById(btnId)?.classList.toggle("active", on);
};
function restoreA11yPreferences() {
const f = localStorage.getItem("a11y_font");
if (f) { window._a11yFontSize = +f; document.documentElement.style.fontSize = f + "%"; }
}
function initPublicNavScrollFX() {
const header = document.querySelector(".header-floating");
const microBar = document.querySelector(".cu-micro-bar");
function onScroll() {
const y = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
if (y > 50) {
if (header) header.classList.add("header-vanished");
if (microBar) microBar.classList.add("header-vanished");
} else {
if (header) header.classList.remove("header-vanished");
if (microBar) microBar.classList.remove("header-vanished");
}
}
window.addEventListener("scroll", onScroll, { passive: true });
onScroll();
}
function initHeroParallax() {
const heroImg = document.querySelector(".hero-image-container > img");
if (!heroImg) return;
if (window.matchMedia("(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)").matches) return;
let ticking = false;
window.addEventListener("scroll", () => {
if (ticking) return;
icking = true;
requestAnimationFrame(() => {
const y = window.scrollY || 0;
const t = Math.min(1, y / 500);
heroImg.style.transform = "scale(" + (1 + t * 0.05) + ") translate3d(0," + (y * 0.06) + "px,0)";
icking = false;
});
}, { passive: true });
}
function initHeroScrollCue() {
document.querySelectorAll(".hero-scroll-cue").forEach((btn) => {
btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
const sel = btn.getAttribute("data-scroll-target") || "#about";
const el = document.querySelector(sel);
el?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
});
});
}

// Chat state
window._chatHistory = [];
window.toggleChatPanel = function() {
const p = document.getElementById("chatPanel");
if (!p) return;
const isActive = p.classList.contains("active");
if (isActive) {
p.classList.remove("active");
setTimeout(() => { p.style.display = "none"; }, 300);
} else {
p.style.display = "flex";
requestAnimationFrame(() => { requestAnimationFrame(() => { p.classList.add("active"); }); });
setTimeout(() => document.getElementById("chatInput")?.focus(), 350);
}
};
window.sendChatMessage = async function() {
const inp = document.getElementById("chatInput");
const msg = inp.value.trim();
if (!msg) return;
appendChatMsg(msg, "user");
inp.value = "";
const loader = document.createElement("div");
loader.className = "loading-msg";
loader.innerHTML = '<div class="typing-indicator"><div class="typing-dot"></div><div class="typing-dot"></div><div class="typing-dot"></div></div>';
const container = document.getElementById("chatMessages");
container.appendChild(loader);
container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;
window._chatHistory.push({ role: "user", parts: [{ text: msg }] });
ry {
let text = "";
// Simulate thinking delay
await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1200));
// Simple keyword mapping for demo chatbot
const lowerMsg = msg.toLowerCase();
const pageText = document.body.innerText.toLowerCase();
if (lowerMsg.includes('admissions') || lowerMsg.includes('apply')) {
ext = "For Admissions (2026-2027), you can check our Admissions page or email us at pgrrdc@gmail.com. We offer BDS, MDS, PhD, and Certificate programs.";
} else if (lowerMsg.includes('appointment') || lowerMsg.includes('book') || lowerMsg.includes('doctor')) {
ext = "To book an appointment, please use the Patient Portal or click the 'Book Appointment' button at the top of the page. Emergency dental care is available 24/7.";
} else if (lowerMsg.includes('contact') || lowerMsg.includes('phone') || lowerMsg.includes('call')) {
ext = "You can reach us at No. 14, Ramohalli Cross, Mysore Road, Bangalore - 560074. Contact number: 080-28437150.";
} else if (lowerMsg.includes('departments') || lowerMsg.includes('courses')) {
ext = "We have 11 specialized departments including Prosthodontics, Orthodontics, Oral Pathology, and more. Use the Department search to explore specific faculty and facilities.";
} else {
// Feed data of the pages: check if word exists in page text
const words = lowerMsg.split(' ').filter(w => w.length > 4);
const matches = words.some(w => pageText.includes(w));
if (matches) {
ext = `I found some information related to your query on this page! Please check the relevant sections or let me know if you need help navigating to specific details like Faculty, Admissions, or Contact info.`;
} else {
ext = "I'm still learning! If you couldn't find what you are looking for, please feel free to navigate our Main Menu or contact the hospital reception directly.";
}
}
loader.remove();
appendChatMsg(text, "bot");
window._chatHistory.push({ role: "model", parts: [{ text: text }] });
if (window._chatHistory.length > 10) window._chatHistory = window._chatHistory.slice(-10);
} catch (e) {
loader.remove();
appendChatMsg("I'm offline right now. Please try again or call 080-28437150.", "bot");
window._chatHistory.pop();
}
};
function appendChatMsg(text, type) {
const container = document.getElementById("chatMessages");
const div = document.createElement("div");
div.className = "chat-msg " + type;
div.textContent = text;
container.appendChild(div);
container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;
return div;
}
========== ./js/utils.js ==========
// js/utils.js
window.RRDCH_UTILS = {
showToast: function(message, type = 'success') {
let toast = document.getElementById("toast");
if (!toast) {
oast = document.createElement("div");
oast.id = "toast";
oast.className = "toast";
document.body.appendChild(toast);
}
oast.textContent = message;
oast.style.background = type === 'success' ? '#22c55e' : (type === 'error' ? '#ef4444' : '#3b82f6');
oast.style.display = "block";
setTimeout(() => toast.style.display = "none", 3000);
},
showElement: function(id) {
const el = document.getElementById(id);
if (el) el.style.display = 'block';
},
hideElement: function(id) {
const el = document.getElementById(id);
if (el) el.style.display = 'none';
},
saveToStorage: function(key, value) {
localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value));
},
getFromStorage: function(key, defaultValue = null) {
const val = localStorage.getItem(key);
return val ? JSON.parse(val) : defaultValue;
}
};
========== ./js/api.js ==========
// js/api.js — Unified AI helper using Gemini REST API directly (no server needed)
(function() {
const GEMINI_KEY = 'AIzaSyBhCpDnWo8u_GdHfu7ermBLbnABuOJVA4U';
const GEMINI_URL = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent?key=${GEMINI_KEY}`;
const RRDCH_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are the official AI assistant for Rajarajeshwari Dental College and Hospital (RRDCH), Bangalore.
Key Facts:
- Address: 14 Ramohalli Cross, Mysore Road, Kumbalgodu, Bangalore 560074
- Phone: 080-28437150
- Email: info@rrdch.org, principalrrdch@gmail.com
- Established: 1992
- Affiliated to RGUHS, Recognized by DCI
- Accreditations: NABH, NAAC A+, ISO 9001:2015
- Courses: BDS (5 years), MDS (3 years), PhD, Certificate courses
- Departments: Oral Surgery, Orthodontics, Periodontology, Conservative Dentistry & Endodontics, Prosthodontics, Oral Medicine & Radiology, Pedodontics, Public Health Dentistry, Implantology, Orofacial Pain, Oral Pathology & Microbiology
- OPD: Monday–Saturday, 9 AM–5 PM
- Emergency dental care: 24/7
- Facilities: 250+ dental chairs, digital X-ray, CBCT scanner, hostel, digital library, gymnasium, sports, transport, Wi-Fi campus
Instructions:
- Keep answers concise (2-3 sentences).
- Be friendly and reassuring.
- If unsure, direct users to call 080-28437150.
- Respond in the same language as the user.
- Never invent information not listed above.`;
/**
* Send a message to Gemini 1.5 Flash directly from the browser.
* @param {string} userMessage
* @param {Array} history
* @param {string|null} systemOverride
* @param {boolean} jsonMode
* @returns {Promise<{text: string, error: string|null}>}
*/
window.askGemini = async function(userMessage, history = [], systemOverride = null, jsonMode = false) {
const systemText = systemOverride || RRDCH_SYSTEM_PROMPT;
const historyText = (history || []).map(h => h.parts?.[0]?.text || '').filter(Boolean).join('\n');
const fullPrompt = jsonMode
? userMessage
: `${systemText}\n\n${historyText ? 'Conversation history:\n' + historyText + '\n\n' : ''}User: ${userMessage}`;
ry {
const res = await fetch(GEMINI_URL, {
method: 'POST',
headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
body: JSON.stringify({
contents: [{ parts: [{ text: fullPrompt }] }],
generationConfig: jsonMode ? { responseMimeType: 'application/json' } : {}
})
});
const data = await res.json();
if (!res.ok || data.error) {
return { text: null, error: data.error?.message || 'Gemini API error' };
}
const text = data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
if (!text) return { text: null, error: 'Empty response from AI.' };
// Log session to Supabase
if (window.sb) {
ry { await window.sb.from('chatbot_sessions').insert({ query: userMessage, response: text, mode: jsonMode ? 'symptom-checker' : 'site-assistant', urgency: 'Routine', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch (_) {}
}
return { text, error: null };
} catch (e) {
return { text: null, error: 'Network error. Please try again.' };
}
};
window.RRDCH_SYSTEM_PROMPT = RRDCH_SYSTEM_PROMPT;
})();

{ time:'11:30 AM', name:'Farhan Iqbal', procedure:'Braces Tightening', type:'upcoming' },
{ time:'12:00 PM', name:'Lakshmi D.', procedure:'Periodontal Checkup', type:'upcoming' },
{ time:'02:00 PM', name:'Walk-in Emergency', procedure:'Trauma / Urgent — TBD', type:'emergency' },
{ time:'04:00 PM', name:'Department Meeting', procedure:'HOD + Residents — OT Block', type:'' },
];
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  STATE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
let queue = [...DEMO_QUEUE];
let savedNotes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('rrdch_case_notes') || '[]');
let currentPage = 'dashboard';
let notifications = [
{ id:1, msg:'Patient #43 Meera Sharma is waiting — Wisdom Tooth Pain', time: new Date(Date.now()-3*60000).toISOString(), read: false },
{ id:2, msg:'New walk-in patient added to queue: Farhan Iqbal', time: new Date(Date.now()-10*60000).toISOString(), read: false },
{ id:3, msg:'Queue auto-refreshed — 4 patients active', time: new Date(Date.now()-20*60000).toISOString(), read: true },
];
let docProfile = { name: 'Dr. Roshan M.', dept: 'Oral Surgery', email: 'doctor@rrdch.in' };
function doLogout() { sessionStorage.removeItem('rrdch_role'); sessionStorage.removeItem('rrdch_user'); if (sb) { try { sb.auth.signOut(); } catch(_){} } }
// Check session
(function checkSession() {
if (sessionStorage.getItem('rrdch_role') !== 'doctor') {
window.location.replace('portal.html#doctor');
} else {
initPortal();
}
})();
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  INIT
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function initPortal() {
updateClock();
setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
const greet = docProfile.name.split(' ').slice(0,2).join(' ') || 'Doctor';
setEl('docGreetName', greet);
setEl('docNameNav', greet);
setEl('docNameSidebar', docProfile.name);
setEl('docDeptSidebar', docProfile.dept);
const initials = docProfile.name.split(' ').filter(w=>w.startsWith('Dr.')||w.length>1).slice(1).map(w=>w[0]).join('').substring(0,2).toUpperCase() || 'DR';
setEl('docInitials', initials);
setEl('docAvatarNav', initials);
document.getElementById('schedDateBadge').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {weekday:'short', month:'short', day:'numeric'});
document.getElementById('schedDateFull').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'});
document.getElementById('dashSubtitle').textContent = 'Clinical summary for ' + new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {weekday:'long', month:'long', day:'numeric'});
loadAllData();
setInterval(() => { loadQueue(); }, 30000);
renderNotifications();
updateNotifBadge();
}
function updateClock() { const el = document.getElementById('navTime'); if (el) el.textContent = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-IN', {hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit', second:'2-digit'}); }
function loadAllData() { loadQueue(); renderSchedule(); loadSavedNotes(); }
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NAVIGATION
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function switchPage(name) {
currentPage = name;
document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
const pg = document.getElementById('page-' + name);
if (pg) pg.classList.add('active');
document.querySelectorAll('.s-link').forEach(l => l.classList.toggle('active', l.dataset.page === name));
window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
if (name === 'notes') loadSavedNotes();
if (name === 'records') searchRecords();
if (name === 'notifications') renderNotifications();
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  QUEUE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadQueue() {
if (sb) {
ry {
const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
const { data, error } = await sb.from('opd_visits').select('*').gte('created_at', today + 'T00:00:00').order('id', { ascending: true });
if (!error && data && data.length > 0) {
queue = data.map(d => ({ ...d, token_no: d.token || d.token_no, reason: d.reason || d.chief_complaint || 'General', time_slot: d.scheduled_at ? new Date(d.scheduled_at).toLocaleTimeString('en-IN',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'}) : 'Walk-in' }));
}
} catch(_) {}
}
updateStats();
renderQueue(queue);
renderNextPatient();
renderSchedule();
updateApptCount();
}
function updateStats() {
const total = queue.length, done = queue.filter(p=>p.status==='done').length;
const waiting = queue.filter(p=>p.status==='waiting'||p.status==='called').length, urgent = 2;
setEl('kpiTotal', total); setEl('kpiDone', done); setEl('kpiWaiting', waiting); setEl('kpiUrgent', urgent);
setEl('queueBadge', queue.filter(p=>p.status==='waiting').length);
}
function renderQueue(q) {
const tbody = document.getElementById('queueTbody');
if (!tbody) return;
if (!q.length) { tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6"><div class="empty"><h3>No patients in queue</h3></div></td></tr>`; return; }
body.innerHTML = q.map(p => {
let actions = '';
if (p.status==='waiting') actions = `<button class="abtn call" onclick="queueAction(${p.id},'called')"><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M22 16.92v3a2 2 0 0 1-2.18 2 19.79 19.79 0 0 1-8.63-3.07A19.5 19.5 0 0 1 4.69 13a19.79 19.79 0 0 1-3.07-8.67A2 2 0 0 1 3.6 2.22h3a2 2 0 0 1 2 1.72c.127.96.361 1.903.7 2.81a2 2 0 0 1-.45 2.11L7.91 9.91a16 16 0 0 0 6 6l.92-.92a2 2 0 0 1 2.11-.45c.907.339 1.85.573 2.81.7A2 2 0 0 1 21.73 17z"/></svg> Call</button>`;
else if (p.status==='called') actions = `<button class="abtn start" onclick="queueAction(${p.id},'ongoing')"><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polygon points="5 3 19 12 5 21 5 3"/></svg> Start</button>`;
else if (p.status==='ongoing') actions = `<button class="abtn done" onclick="queueAction(${p.id},'done')"><svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg> Done</button><button class="abtn view" onclick="addNoteForPatient('${p.token_no}','${p.patient_name}')">Note</button>`;
else actions = '<span style="color:var(--muted);font-size:0.8rem;">✓ Complete</span>';
return `<tr id="qrow-${p.id}"><td><span class="token">${p.token_no}</span></td><td><strong>${p.patient_name}</strong><br><span style="font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--muted);">${p.phone||'—'}</span></td><td>${p.reason||'General'}</td><td>${p.time_slot||'Walk-in'}</td><td><span class="stag ${p.status}">${capitalize(p.status)}</span></td><td><div style="display:flex;gap:0.4rem;">${actions}</div></td></tr>`;
}).join('');
}
function filterQueue() {
const q = document.getElementById('qSearch').value.toLowerCase();
const st = document.getElementById('qStatusFilter').value;
renderQueue(queue.filter(p => {
const m = !q || (p.patient_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.token_no||'').includes(q) || (p.reason||'').toLowerCase().includes(q);
const sm = !st || p.status === st;
return m && sm;
}));
}
async function queueAction(id, newStatus) {
const p = queue.find(x => x.id === id); if (!p) return;
p.status = newStatus;
if (sb) { try { await sb.from('opd_visits').update({ status: newStatus, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('id', id); } catch(_){} }
updateStats(); filterQueue(); renderNextPatient();
addNotification(`Patient ${p.patient_name} (${p.token_no}) → ${capitalize(newStatus)}`);
if (newStatus === 'ongoing') addNoteForPatient(p.token_no, p.patient_name);
showToast(`✓ ${p.patient_name} marked as ${capitalize(newStatus)}`, 'success');
}
function renderNextPatient() {
const next = queue.find(p => p.status === 'waiting' || p.status === 'called' || p.status === 'ongoing');
const el = document.getElementById('nextPatientWidget');
const badge = document.getElementById('nextBadge');
if (!next || !el) return;
badge.textContent = next.token_no;
el.innerHTML = `
<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:0.75rem;padding:0.25rem;">
<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:1rem;">
<div style="width:52px;height:52px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--blue);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:white;font-size:1.25rem;font-weight:800;">${next.patient_name[0]}</div>
<div><strong style="font-size:1.05rem;">${next.patient_name}</strong><br><span style="font-size:0.78rem;color:var(--muted);">${next.phone||'—'} • ${next.time_slot}</span></div>
</div>
<div style="background:var(--bg);border-radius:8px;padding:0.75rem;">
<div style="font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:0.25rem;">CHIEF COMPLAINT</div>
<div style="font-weight:600;">${next.reason||'General Consultation'}</div>
</div>
<div style="display:flex;gap:0.5rem;">
${next.status==='waiting'?`<button class="abtn call" onclick="queueAction(${next.id},'called');switchPage('queue')">📞 Call Patient</button>`:''}
${next.status==='called'?`<button class="abtn start" onclick="queueAction(${next.id},'ongoing');switchPage('queue')">▶ Start Consultation</button>`:''}
${next.status==='ongoing'?`<button class="abtn done" onclick="queueAction(${next.id},'done');switchPage('queue')">✓ Mark Done</button><button class="abtn view" onclick="addNoteForPatient('${next.token_no}','${next.patient_name}');switchPage('notes')">📝 Add Note</button>`:''}
</div>
<span class="stag ${next.status}" style="align-self:flex-start;">${capitalize(next.status)}</span>
</div>`;
}
function updateApptCount() { document.getElementById('queueBadge').textContent = queue.filter(p=>p.status==='waiting').length; }
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SCHEDULE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function renderSchedule() {
const items = DEMO_SCHEDULE;
const html = items.map(s => `
<div class="si ${s.type}">
<div class="si-time">${s.time}</div>
<div>
<div class="si-name" ${s.type==='emergency'?'style="color:var(--red);"':''}>${s.name}</div>
<div class="si-dept">${s.procedure}</div>
</div>
${s.type==='upcoming'?'<span class="stag called" style="margin-left:auto;font-size:0.65rem;">Scheduled</span>':''}
${s.type==='done-slot'?'<span class="stag done" style="margin-left:auto;font-size:0.65rem;">Done</span>':''}
${s.type==='emergency'?'<span class="stag ongoing" style="margin-left:auto;font-size:0.65rem;background:#fee2e2;color:#991b1b;">Urgent</span>':''}
</div>`).join('');
const ep = document.getElementById('schedPreview');
const fp = document.getElementById('fullSchedule');
if (ep) ep.innerHTML = html;
if (fp) fp.innerHTML = html;
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CASE NOTES
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function saveNote() {
const patient     = document.getElementById('notePatient').value.trim();
const diagnosis   = document.getElementById('noteDiagnosis').value.trim();
const treatment   = document.getElementById('noteTreatment').value.trim();
const prescription= document.getElementById('notePrescription').value.trim();
const content     = document.getElementById('noteContent').value.trim();
if (!patient || !diagnosis) { showToast('Patient and Diagnosis are required', 'error'); return; }
const btn = document.getElementById('noteSaveBtn');
btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner"></div> Saving…';
btn.disabled = true;
const note = { id: Date.now(), patient, diagnosis, treatment, prescription, content, doctor: docProfile.name, dept: docProfile.dept, created_at: new Date().toISOString() };
if (sb) { try { await sb.from('case_notes').insert({ patient_info: patient, diagnosis, treatment, prescription, notes: content, doctor_name: docProfile.name, department: docProfile.dept, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch(_){} }
savedNotes.unshift(note);
localStorage.setItem('rrdch_case_notes', JSON.stringify(savedNotes.slice(0, 50)));
btn.innerHTML = '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg> Saved!';
btn.style.background = 'var(--green)';
setTimeout(() => {
btn.innerHTML = '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M19 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11l5 5v11a2 2 0 0 1-2 2z"/><polyline points="17 21 17 13 7 13 7 21"/><polyline points="7 3 7 8 15 8"/></svg> Save Case Note';
btn.style.background = ''; btn.disabled = false;
}, 2000);
loadSavedNotes();
showToast('✓ Case note saved', 'success');
}
function clearNoteForm() {
['notePatient','noteDiagnosis','noteTreatment','notePrescription','noteContent'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.value = ''; });
}
function addNoteForPatient(token, name) {
const el = document.getElementById('notePatient');
if (el) el.value = `${token} — ${name}`;
switchPage('notes');
}
function loadSavedNotes() {
savedNotes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('rrdch_case_notes') || '[]');
const el = document.getElementById('savedNotesContainer');
if (!el) return;
if (!savedNotes.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><p>No notes saved yet.</p></div>'; return; }
el.innerHTML = savedNotes.slice(0, 10).map(n => `
<div class="hist-card">
<div class="hist-date">${new Date(n.created_at).toLocaleString('en-IN')} — ${n.doctor}</div>
<h4>${n.patient}</h4>
<p><strong>Dx:</strong> ${n.diagnosis}</p>
${n.treatment ? `<p><strong>Rx:</strong> ${n.treatment}</p>` : ''}
${n.prescription ? `<p style="margin-top:0.3rem;font-style:italic;">${n.prescription}</p>` : ''}
</div>`).join('');
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  PATIENT RECORDS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function searchRecords() {
const q = (document.getElementById('recordSearch')?.value || '').toLowerCase();
const records = queue.filter(p => !q || (p.patient_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.phone||'').includes(q));
const tbody = document.getElementById('recordsTbody');
if (!tbody) return;
if (!records.length) { tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6"><div class="empty"><h3>No records found</h3></div></td></tr>`; return; }
body.innerHTML = records.map(p => `
<tr>
<td><strong>${p.patient_name}</strong></td>
<td>${p.phone||'—'}</td>
<td>${p.time_slot||'—'}</td>
<td>${p.reason||'—'}</td>
<td><span class="stag ${p.status}">${capitalize(p.status)}</span></td>
<td>
<button class="abtn view" onclick="addNoteForPatient('${p.token_no}','${p.patient_name}');switchPage('notes')">Add Note</button>
</td>
</tr>`).join('');
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  AI ASSISTANT
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
async function sendAIMessage() {
const input = document.getElementById('chatInput');
const msg = input.value.trim();
if (!msg) return;
input.value = '';
const msgs = document.getElementById('chatMessages');
msgs.innerHTML += `<div class="msg user">${escapeHtml(msg)}</div>`;
msgs.innerHTML += `<div class="msg bot thinking" id="thinking">⏳ Thinking…</div>`;
msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;
ry {
const isSymptom = msg.toLowerCase().includes('pain') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('bleed') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('swelling') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('ache') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('extraction') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('tooth');
const mode = isSymptom ? 'symptom-checker' : 'clinical-assistant';
const prompt = mode === 'symptom-checker'
? `You are a dental clinical assistant for a dentist at RRDCH Bangalore. The dentist says: "${msg}". Provide a concise clinical assessment including: possible diagnosis, recommended treatment, and any urgent considerations. Be specific and clinical.`
: `You are an expert dental clinical assistant. The dentist at RRDCH asks: "${msg}". Provide a precise, practical clinical answer. Use plain text, be concise, and focus on actionable advice.`;
const res = await fetch(`https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent?key=${GEMINI_KEY}`, {
method: 'POST',
headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
body: JSON.stringify({ contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }] })
});
const data = await res.json();
let text = data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || 'I could not generate a response. Please try again.';
ext = text.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>').replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
const thinking = document.getElementById('thinking');
if (thinking) thinking.outerHTML = `<div class="msg bot">${text}</div>`;
// Save to chatbot_sessions
if (sb) { try { await sb.from('chatbot_sessions').insert({ query: msg, mode: 'clinical-assistant', urgency: 'Routine', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch(_){} }
} catch(err) {
const thinking = document.getElementById('thinking');
if (thinking) thinking.outerHTML = `<div class="msg bot">⚠️ AI request failed. Please check your connection.</div>`;
}
msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;
}
function setPrompt(text) { document.getElementById('chatInput').value = text; document.getElementById('chatInput').focus(); }
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NOTIFICATIONS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function addNotification(msg) {
notifications.unshift({ id: Date.now(), msg, time: new Date().toISOString(), read: false });
updateNotifBadge();
}
function updateNotifBadge() {
const unread = notifications.filter(n => !n.read).length;
const dot = document.getElementById('notifDot');
if (dot) dot.style.display = unread > 0 ? 'block' : 'none';
}
function renderNotifications() {
const el = document.getElementById('notifList');
if (!el) return;
if (!notifications.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><div class="empty"><h3>No notifications</h3></div></div>'; return; }
el.innerHTML = notifications.map(n => `
<div class="card" style="margin-bottom:0.75rem;padding:1rem 1.25rem;border-left:4px solid ${n.read?'var(--border)':'var(--blue)'};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:1rem;">
<div>
<div style="font-size:0.88rem;font-weight:${n.read?'500':'700'};color:${n.read?'var(--muted)':'var(--text)'};">${n.msg}</div>
<div style="font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--muted);margin-top:0.25rem;">${timeAgo(n.time)}</div>
</div>
${!n.read?`<button style="background:none;border:none;font-size:0.75rem;color:var(--blue);font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:inherit;padding:0.25rem 0.5rem;" onclick="markRead(${n.id})">Mark Read</button>`:''}
</div>`).join('');
notifications.forEach(n => n.read = true);
updateNotifBadge();
}
function markRead(id) { const n = notifications.find(x=>x.id===id); if(n) n.read=true; renderNotifications(); updateNotifBadge(); }
function clearNotifications() { notifications.forEach(n=>n.read=true); renderNotifications(); updateNotifBadge(); showToast('All notifications cleared','success'); }
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
//  UTILS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function setEl(id, val) { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = val; }
function capitalize(s) { return s ? s.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s.slice(1) : ''; }
function timeAgo(ts) { const d=Math.floor((Date.now()-new Date(ts).getTime())/1000); if(d<60)return'just now'; if(d<3600)return Math.floor(d/60)+'m ago'; if(d<86400)return Math.floor(d/3600)+'h ago'; return new Date(ts).toLocaleDateString('en-IN'); }
function escapeHtml(s) { return s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function showToast(msg, type='') { const t=document.getElementById('toast'); t.textContent=msg; t.className='toast show '+type; clearTimeout(t._t); t._t=setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'),3000); }
</script>
</body>
</html>

} catch(e) { console.warn('Supabase init error:', e); }

// ======================
// PARTICLES

(function spawnParticles() {
const container = document.getElementById('particles');
for (let i = 0; i < 18; i++) {
const p = document.createElement('div');
p.className = 'p';
p.style.cssText = `left:${Math.random()*100}%;width:${2+Math.random()*3}px;height:${2+Math.random()*3}px;animation-duration:${10+Math.random()*15}s;animation-delay:${Math.random()*10}s;opacity:${0.3+Math.random()*0.5};`;
container.appendChild(p);
}
})();
// ======================
// ROLE SWITCHING
// ======================
function switchRole(role) {
currentRole = role;
// Update tabs
document.querySelectorAll('.role-tab').forEach(t => {
.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.role === role);
});
renderLoginCard(role);
showLogin();
}
function renderLoginCard(role) {
const cfg = ROLES[role];
const fieldsHtml = cfg.fields.map(f =>
`<input type="${f.type}" id="${f.id}" class="flip-card__input" placeholder="${f.placeholder}" required>`
).join('');
const signupLink = cfg.showSignup
? `<button class="card-link" onclick="showSignup()">New patient? Register →</button>`
: `<span style="font-size:0.72rem;color:#94a3b8;">Staff login only</span>`;
document.getElementById('loginCard').innerHTML = `
<div class="role-badge ${cfg.badge}">${cfg.badgeText}</div>
<div class="card-title">${cfg.title}</div>
<div class="card-sub">${cfg.sub}</div>
${cfg.demoHtml}
<form id="loginForm" onsubmit="handleLogin(event, '${role}')" novalidate>
<div class="form-group">${fieldsHtml}</div>
<div class="error-box" id="${cfg.errorId}">
<svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><line x1="12" y1="8" x2="12" y2="12"/></svg>
<span id="${cfg.errorId}Msg">Invalid credentials. Please try again.</span>
</div>
<button type="submit" class="login-btn" id="loginBtn">
<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg>
Sign In
</button>
</form>
<div class="card-links">
${signupLink}
<button class="card-link" onclick="alert('Please contact RRDCH IT support at it@rrdch.in')">Forgot Password?</button>
</div>
`;
}
// ======================
// SHOW / HIDE FORMS
// ======================
function showSignup() {
document.getElementById('loginCardWrap').style.display = 'none';
document.getElementById('signupCardWrap').style.display = 'block';
}
function showLogin() {
document.getElementById('loginCardWrap').style.display = 'block';
document.getElementById('signupCardWrap').style.display = 'none';
}
// ======================
// LOGIN HANDLER
// ======================
async function handleLogin(e, role) {
e.preventDefault();
const cfg = ROLES[role];
const demo = DEMO[role];
const errDiv  = document.getElementById(cfg.errorId);
const errMsg  = document.getElementById(cfg.errorId + 'Msg');
const btn     = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
errDiv.classList.remove('show');
btn.disabled = true;
btn.innerHTML = `<div class="spinner" style="width:20px;height:20px;border-width:3px;"></div> Signing in…`;
// Gather credentials
let identifier = '', password = '';
if (role === 'patient') {
identifier = document.getElementById('patId')?.value.trim();
password   = document.getElementById('patPw')?.value;
} else if (role === 'doctor') {
identifier = document.getElementById('docEmail')?.value.trim().toLowerCase();
password   = document.getElementById('docPw')?.value;
} else if (role === 'student') {
identifier = document.getElementById('stuId')?.value.trim();
password   = document.getElementById('stuPw')?.value;
} else if (role === 'admin') {
identifier = document.getElementById('admEmail')?.value.trim().toLowerCase();
password   = document.getElementById('admPw')?.value;
}
let success = false;
let redirectUrl = demo.redirect;
// — Try Supabase auth first (email/password roles) —
if (sb && (role === 'doctor' || role === 'admin')) {
ry {
const timeoutPromise = new Promise((_, reject) => setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('timeout')), 2500));
const { data, error } = await Promise.race([
sb.auth.signInWithPassword({ email: identifier, password }),
imeoutPromise
]);
if (!error && data?.user) {
success = true;
// Log the login event
ry { await sb.from('admin_audit_log').insert({ role, user_email: identifier, action: 'login', status: 'success' }); } catch(_) {}
}
} catch(ex) { console.warn('Supabase auth error or timeout falling back to demo:', ex); }
}
// — Demo fallback —
if (!success) {
if (role === 'patient'  && (identifier === demo.credential || identifier === 'patient@rrdch.in') && password === demo.password) success = true;
if (role === 'doctor'   && identifier === demo.email  && password === demo.password) success = true;
if (role === 'student'  && (identifier === demo.credential || identifier === demo.email) && password === demo.password) success = true;
if (role === 'admin'    && identifier === demo.email  && password === demo.password) success = true;
}
if (success) {
// Store session
sessionStorage.setItem('rrdch_role', role);
sessionStorage.setItem('rrdch_user', identifier);
sessionStorage.setItem('rrdch_login_time', new Date().toISOString());
showToast(`✓ Welcome! Redirecting to ${role} portal…`);
showSpinner('Loading your portal…');
await delay(1000);
window.location.href = redirectUrl;
} else {
errMsg.textContent = 'Invalid credentials. Please check and try again.';
errDiv.classList.add('show');
btn.disabled = false;
btn.innerHTML = `<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M15 3h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2h-4"/><polyline points="10 17 15 12 10 7"/><line x1="15" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"/></svg> Sign In`;
// Shake the card
document.getElementById('loginCard').style.animation = 'none';
setTimeout(() => { document.getElementById('loginCard').style.animation = ''; }, 50);
}
}
// ======================
// PATIENT REGISTRATION
// ======================
async function handleRegister() {
const name  = document.getElementById('regName').value.trim();
const email = document.getElementById('regEmail').value.trim();
const phone = document.getElementById('regPhone').value.trim();
const pw    = document.getElementById('regPw').value;
const errDiv = document.getElementById('regError');
const errMsg = document.getElementById('regErrorMsg');
const btn    = document.getElementById('regBtn');
errDiv.classList.remove('show');
if (!name || !email || !phone || !pw) { errMsg.textContent = 'All fields are required.'; errDiv.classList.add('show'); return; }
if (pw.length < 6) { errMsg.textContent = 'Password must be at least 6 characters.'; errDiv.classList.add('show'); return; }
btn.disabled = true;
btn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner" style="width:20px;height:20px;border-width:3px;"></div> Creating account…';
let success = false;
if (sb) {
ry {
const { data, error } = await sb.auth.signUp({ email, password: pw, options: { data: { full_name: name, phone, role: 'patient' } } });
if (!error) {
success = true;
ry { await sb.from('patients').insert({ name, email, phone, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }); } catch(_) {}
} else {
errMsg.textContent = error.message || 'Registration failed.';
errDiv.classList.add('show');
}
} catch(ex) { errMsg.textContent = 'Network error. Please try again.'; errDiv.classList.add('show'); }
} else {
// Demo mode: just show success
success = true;
}
if (success) {
showToast('✓ Account created! Please check your email to verify, then login.');
await delay(2500);
showLogin();
}
btn.disabled = false;
btn.innerHTML = `<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M16 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-4-4H6a4 4 0 0 0-4 4v2"/><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="4"/><line x1="19" y1="8" x2="19" y2="14"/><line x1="22" y1="11" x2="16" y2="11"/></svg> Register`;
}
// ======================
// UTILS
// ======================
function showToast(msg) {
const t = document.getElementById('toast');
.innerHTML = `<svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg> ${msg}`;
.classList.add('show');
setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 4000);
}
function showSpinner(msg) {
document.getElementById('spinnerText').textContent = msg || 'Loading…';
document.getElementById('spinnerOverlay').classList.add('show');
}
function delay(ms) { return new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms)); }
// ======================
// URL HASH ROLE SELECTION
// ======================
function initFromHash() {
const hash = window.location.hash.replace('#','').toLowerCase();
const validRoles = ['patient','doctor','student','admin'];
if (validRoles.includes(hash)) {
switchRole(hash);
} else {
switchRole('patient');
}
}
// ======================
// INIT
// ======================
initFromHash();
window.addEventListener('hashchange', initFromHash);
</script>
</body>
</html>
========== ./supabase/schema.sql ==========
-- RRDCH Full Schema — Updated for portal integration
-- Run this in Supabase SQL Editor
-- ─── OPD Queue (public summary) ───────────────────────────────────────
create table if not exists public.opd_queue (
id                bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
department        text not null,
doctor_name       text,
current_token     text,
otal_waiting     integer default 0,
est_wait_minutes  integer default 0,
status            text default 'open',
updated_at        timestamptz default now()
);
-- ─── OPD Visits / Appointments ────────────────────────────────────────
create table if not exists public.opd_visits (
id            bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
oken         text,
department    text not null,
patient_name  text not null,
age           integer,
phone         text,
reason        text,
doctor_name   text,
status        text default 'waiting',
notes         text,
scheduled_at  timestamptz default now(),
created_at    timestamptz default now(),
updated_at    timestamptz default now()
);
-- ─── Patients ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
create table if not exists public.patients (
id           bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
name         text not null,
email        text,
phone        text,
age          integer,
patient_id   text,
status       text default 'active',
last_visit   date,
created_at   timestamptz default now()
);
-- ─── Case Notes ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
create table if not exists public.case_notes (
id            bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
patient_info  text,
diagnosis     text,
reatment     text,
prescription  text,
notes         text,
doctor_name   text,
department    text,
oken_no      text,
created_at    timestamptz default now()
);
-- ─── Chatbot Sessions ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
create table if not exists public.chatbot_sessions (
id              bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
session_id      text,
query           text,
response        text,
mode            text,
urgency         text default 'Routine',
department      text,
user_role       text default 'patient',
created_at      timestamptz default now()
);
-- ─── Admin Audit Log ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
create table if not exists public.admin_audit_log (
id           bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
user_email   text,
role         text,
action       text,
status       text default 'success',
ip           text,
created_at   timestamptz default now()
);
-- ─── RLS Policies ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
alter table public.opd_queue          enable row level security;
alter table public.opd_visits         enable row level security;
alter table public.patients           enable row level security;
alter table public.case_notes         enable row level security;
alter table public.chatbot_sessions   enable row level security;
alter table public.admin_audit_log    enable row level security;
-- Public read for queue summary (patient-facing queue display)
drop policy if exists "public read opd_queue" on public.opd_queue;
create policy "public read opd_queue" on public.opd_queue
for select to anon using (true);
-- Allow anon inserts for chatbot sessions
drop policy if exists "anon insert chatbot" on public.chatbot_sessions;
create policy "anon insert chatbot" on public.chatbot_sessions
for insert to anon with check (true);
-- Allow anon inserts for audit log (login events)
drop policy if exists "anon insert audit" on public.admin_audit_log;
create policy "anon insert audit" on public.admin_audit_log
for insert to anon with check (true);
-- Allow anon inserts for patient registration
drop policy if exists "anon insert patients" on public.patients;
create policy "anon insert patients" on public.patients
for insert to anon with check (true);
-- Allow anon inserts for appointment booking
drop policy if exists "anon insert visits" on public.opd_visits;
create policy "anon insert visits" on public.opd_visits
for insert to anon with check (true);
-- Allow anon read of visits (for doctor portal demo)
drop policy if exists "anon read visits" on public.opd_visits;
create policy "anon read visits" on public.opd_visits
for select to anon using (true);
-- Allow anon update of visit status (queue actions)
drop policy if exists "anon update visits" on public.opd_visits;
create policy "anon update visits" on public.opd_visits
for update to anon using (true);
-- Allow anon insert for case notes
drop policy if exists "anon insert notes" on public.case_notes;
create policy "anon insert notes" on public.case_notes
for insert to anon with check (true);
-- Allow anon read of patients
drop policy if exists "anon read patients" on public.patients;
create policy "anon read patients" on public.patients
for select to anon using (true);
-- Realtime for patient queue and visits
alter publication supabase_realtime add table public.opd_queue;
alter publication supabase_realtime add table public.opd_visits;
-- ─── Seed demo data (opd_visits) ──────────────────────────────────────
insert into public.opd_visits (token, department, patient_name, phone, reason, status, scheduled_at)

========== ./supabase/public_site.sql ==========
-- Public site form storage (used by Vercel functions with service role key).
create table if not exists public.contact_enquiries (
id bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
name text not null,
email text not null,
phone text,
subject text,
message text not null,
created_at timestamptz default now()
);
create table if not exists public.admission_enquiries (
id bigint generated by default as identity primary key,
name text not null,
phone text not null,
email text not null,
course text not null,
query text not null,
status text default 'new',
created_at timestamptz default now()
);
alter table public.contact_enquiries enable row level security;
alter table public.admission_enquiries enable row level security;
-- Public inserts allowed (optional; you can also keep inserts server-only by removing these policies).
drop policy if exists "public insert contact" on public.contact_enquiries;
create policy "public insert contact"
on public.contact_enquiries for insert
o anon
with check (true);
drop policy if exists "public insert admissions" on public.admission_enquiries;
create policy "public insert admissions"
on public.admission_enquiries for insert
o anon
with check (true);
-- Public select denied.
drop policy if exists "deny public select contact" on public.contact_enquiries;
create policy "deny public select contact"
on public.contact_enquiries for select
o anon
using (false);
drop policy if exists "deny public select admissions" on public.admission_enquiries;
create policy "deny public select admissions"
on public.admission_enquiries for select
o anon
using (false);

<script>
lucide.createIcons();
// Time Slot Logic
let selT = null;
function selTime(el) {
document.querySelectorAll('.time-slot').forEach(e => e.classList.remove('selected'));
el.classList.add('selected');
selT = el.textContent;
}
const sb = window.sb || (window.RRDCH_CONFIG && window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_URL && !window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_URL.startsWith("YOUR_")
? supabase.createClient(window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_URL, window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_ANON_KEY)
: null);
function loadQueue() {
if(!sb) return;
sb.from("opd_queue").select("*").order("department").then(({data, error}) => {
if(error || !data) return;
const container = document.getElementById("liveQueueContainer");
container.innerHTML = "";
data.forEach(row => {
const waitNum = row.est_wait_minutes;
let dotCol = "#22c55e";
if(waitNum >= 10 && waitNum <= 20) dotCol = "#eab308";
else if(waitNum > 20) dotCol = "#ef4444";
container.innerHTML += `
<div class="queue-item">
<div>
<div style="font-weight:600; font-size:1.05rem; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:0.4rem;">
<span style="width:8px; height:8px; border-radius:50%; background:${dotCol}; display:inline-block;"></span>
${row.department}</div>
<span style="font-size:0.8rem; color:#94a3b8;">${row.doctor_name || 'Doctor'} • Est. Wait: ${waitNum} min</span>
</div>
<div class="queue-token">#${row.current_token}</div>
</div>`;
});
});
}
if (sb) {
sb.channel("queue-changes").on("postgres_changes", { event: "*", schema: "public", table: "opd_queue" }, () => loadQueue()).subscribe();
loadQueue();
} else {
const container = document.getElementById("liveQueueContainer");
if (container) {
container.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:0.9rem;border:1px dashed #cbd5e1;border-radius:10px;color:#64748b;">Live queue is unavailable. Configure Supabase in <code>js/config.js</code>.</div>';
}
}
async function analyseSymptoms() {
const input = document.getElementById("symptomInput").value.trim();
if(!input) { alert("Please describe your symptoms first."); return; }
document.getElementById("symptomLoading").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("symptomResult").style.display = "none";
ry {
const parsed = await window.RRDCH_AI.askJson(
"You are a dental triage assistant for RRDCH hospital in Bangalore. A patient describes their problem: " +
input +
". Respond ONLY with a JSON object with these exact keys: condition (string, plain language, max 10 words), department (one of: Oral Surgery, Orthodontics, General Dentistry, Periodontology, Pedodontics, Conservative Dentistry and Endodontics, Oral Medicine and Radiology, Implantology), urgency (one of: Routine, Soon, Urgent, Emergency), advice (2 sentences max, plain language, reassuring tone). Return only raw JSON, no markdown."
);
document.getElementById("symCondition").textContent = parsed.condition;
document.getElementById("symDept").textContent = parsed.department;
document.getElementById("symAdvice").textContent = parsed.advice;
const urgEl = document.getElementById("symUrgency");
urgEl.textContent = parsed.urgency;
urgEl.style.color = "white";
if(parsed.urgency === "Routine") { urgEl.style.background = "#22c55e"; }
else if(parsed.urgency === "Soon") { urgEl.style.background = "#eab308"; urgEl.style.color = "#854d0e"; }
else if(parsed.urgency === "Urgent") { urgEl.style.background = "#f97316"; }
else if(parsed.urgency === "Emergency") { urgEl.style.background = "#ef4444"; }
else { urgEl.style.background = "#94a3b8"; }
const deptSelect = document.querySelector('#bookingForm select[required]');
if(deptSelect) {
for(let i=0; i<deptSelect.options.length; i++) {
if(deptSelect.options[i].value.toLowerCase().includes(parsed.department.toLowerCase())) {
deptSelect.selectedIndex = i; break;
}
}
}
document.getElementById("symptomLoading").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("symptomResult").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("symptomResult").style.animation = "pulse 0.5s ease 1";
document.getElementById("symCondition").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("symDept").style.display = "block";
urgEl.style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("symAdvice").style.color = "#475569";
} catch (err) {
document.getElementById("symptomLoading").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("symptomResult").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("symCondition").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("symDept").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("symUrgency").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("symAdvice").textContent = "Could not analyse symptoms. Please try again.";
document.getElementById("symAdvice").style.color = "red";
}
}
const COST_DATA = {
"Routine Checkup & Cleaning": { min:500, max:1200, sessions:1, insurance:false, emi:false, department:"General Dentistry" },
"Tooth Extraction (Simple)": { min:500, max:1500, sessions:1, insurance:true, emi:false, department:"Oral Surgery" },
"Tooth Extraction (Surgical)": { min:2000, max:5000, sessions:1, insurance:true, emi:false, department:"Oral Surgery" },
"Root Canal Treatment (RCT)": { min:3000, max:8000, sessions:3, insurance:true, emi:true, department:"Conservative Dentistry and Endodontics" },
"Dental Crown (Ceramic)": { min:4000, max:10000, sessions:2, insurance:false, emi:true, department:"Prosthodontics" },
"Dental Implant": { min:25000, max:60000, sessions:4, insurance:false, emi:true, department:"Implantology" },
"Braces (Metal)": { min:20000, max:35000, sessions:12, insurance:false, emi:true, department:"Orthodontics" },
"Braces (Ceramic)": { min:30000, max:50000, sessions:12, insurance:false, emi:true, department:"Orthodontics" },
"Invisible Aligners": { min:60000, max:120000, sessions:10, insurance:false, emi:true, department:"Orthodontics" },
"Teeth Whitening": { min:3000, max:8000, sessions:1, insurance:false, emi:false, department:"General Dentistry" },
"Gum Treatment (Scaling)": { min:800, max:2500, sessions:2, insurance:false, emi:false, department:"Periodontology" },
"Dentures (Full)": { min:8000, max:25000, sessions:3, insurance:false, emi:true, department:"Prosthodontics" },
"Composite Filling": { min:800, max:2500, sessions:1, insurance:false, emi:false, department:"Conservative Dentistry and Endodontics" },
"Pediatric Dental Checkup": { min:300, max:800, sessions:1, insurance:false, emi:false, department:"Pedodontics" }
};
document.getElementById("treatmentSelect")?.addEventListener("change", function() {
const val = this.value; const resEl = document.getElementById("costResult");
if(!val || !COST_DATA[val]) { resEl.style.display = "none"; return; }
const data = COST_DATA[val];
document.getElementById("costRange").textContent = `₹${data.min.toLocaleString("en-IN")} – ₹${data.max.toLocaleString("en-IN")}`;
document.getElementById("costSessions").textContent = `${data.sessions} Session${data.sessions > 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
document.getElementById("costInsurance").innerHTML = data.insurance ? "<span style='color:#16a34a;'>✓ May be covered</span>" : "<span style='color:#64748b;'>✗ Self-pay only</span>";
document.getElementById("costPayment").textContent = data.emi ? "EMI available + Cash + Card" : "Cash + Card only";
const deptSelect = document.querySelector('#bookingForm select[required]');
if(deptSelect && data.department) {
for(let i=0; i<deptSelect.options.length; i++) {
if(deptSelect.options[i].value.toLowerCase().includes(data.department.toLowerCase())) { deptSelect.selectedIndex = i; break; }
}
}
resEl.style.display = "block";
});
let feedbackScore = 0;
// Booking Submission (backend-enabled with graceful fallback)
async function submitBooking() {
if(!selT) { alert("Please select a time slot!"); return; }
const form = document.getElementById('bookingForm');
const alertBox = document.getElementById('bookSuccess');
const name = form.querySelector('input[type="text"]').value.trim();
const phone = form.querySelector('input[type="tel"]')?.value.trim() || "";
const dept = form.querySelector('select').value;
const dateInput = form.querySelector('input[type="date"]')?.value;
const date = dateInput ? new Date(dateInput) : new Date();
const dateStr = date.toLocaleDateString("en-IN", {day:"2-digit", month:"short", year:"numeric"});
const time = selT || "10:00 AM";
let tokenNum = Math.floor(Math.random() * 80) + 20;
// Try backend booking first.
ry {
const booked = await fetch("/api/book", {
method: "POST",
headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
body: JSON.stringify({
patientName: name || "Patient",
department: dept,
doctor: form.querySelectorAll("select")[1]?.value || "Doctor",
date: dateInput || new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),
ime,
reason: document.getElementById("symptomInput")?.value.trim() || "",
phone: phone || ""
})
}).then(r => r.json());
if (booked?.ok) {
const tokenRaw = booked.data?.appointment?.token || "";
const tokenDigits = String(tokenRaw).replace(/\D/g, "");
if (tokenDigits) tokenNum = parseInt(tokenDigits, 10);
}
} catch (e) {
window.RRDCH_UTILS?.showToast("Booked in offline mode (backend unavailable).", "info");
}
document.getElementById("tcToken").textContent = "#" + tokenNum;
document.getElementById("tcTokenSmall").textContent = "#" + tokenNum;
document.getElementById("tcName").textContent = name;
document.getElementById("tcDept").textContent = dept;
document.getElementById("tcDate").textContent = dateStr;
document.getElementById("tcTime").textContent = time;
const canvas = document.getElementById("tokenQR");
QRCode.toCanvas(canvas, `RRDCH|Token:${tokenNum}|${dept}|${name}|${dateStr}|${time}`, { width: 150, margin: 1, color: { dark: "#1A365D", light: "#FFFFFF" } });
form.style.display = 'none';
alertBox.style.display = 'flex';
document.getElementById("tokenCard").style.display = "block";
document.getElementById("tokenCard").scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
setTimeout(() => { form.reset(); selT=null; document.querySelectorAll('.time-slot').forEach(e=>e.classList.remove('selected')); }, 3000);
}
function printToken() {
const content = document.getElementById("tokenCardInner").outerHTML;
const win = window.open("", "_blank");
win.document.write(`<html><head><title>RRDCH Token</title><style>body{margin:2rem;font-family:Arial;}</style></head><body>${content}<script>window.print();<\/script></body></html>`);
win.document.close();
}
// Tracker (backend-enabled)
async function processTrack() {
const val = document.getElementById('trackInput').value.trim();
if(!val) return;
const res = document.getElementById('trackerResult');
ry {
const data = val.toUpperCase().includes("A-")
? await window.RRDCH_BACKEND.trackVisit({ token: val })
: await window.RRDCH_BACKEND.trackVisit({ phone: val });
const top = data.data || {};
res.innerHTML = `<strong>Status:</strong> ${top?.status || "Booked"}<br><strong>Token:</strong> ${top?.token || val}<br><strong>Department:</strong> ${top?.department || "--"}<br><strong>Date:</strong> ${top?.scheduled_at || "--"}`;
} catch (e) {
res.innerHTML = "Could not fetch live status right now. Please try again shortly.";
}
res.style.display = 'block';
res.style.animation = 'pulse 0.5s ease 1';
}
// Feedback (backend-enabled)
function rate(num) {
feedbackScore = num;
const stars = document.querySelectorAll('.star-rating');
stars.forEach((s, i) => { s.style.color = i < num ? '#eab308' : '#cbd5e1'; s.style.fill = i < num ? '#eab308' : 'none'; });
}
async function submitFeedback() {
const comment = document.querySelector('#feedbackForm textarea')?.value.trim() || "";
ry {
await window.RRDCH_BACKEND.request("/feedback", {
method: "POST",
body: JSON.stringify({
feedback_type: "patient_portal",
ratings_json: { stars: feedbackScore || 0 },
comment
})
});
} catch (e) {
// Keep UI success even if backend fails in demo mode.
}
document.getElementById('feedbackForm').style.display='none';
document.getElementById('feedSuccess').style.display='flex';
}
// Language Toggle Dictionary Logic
let curLang = 'en';
function toggleLang() {
curLang = curLang === 'en' ? 'kn' : 'en';
document.getElementById('enBtn').className = curLang === 'en' ? 'active' : '';
document.getElementById('enBtn').style.opacity = curLang === 'en' ? '1' : '0.5';
document.getElementById('knBtn').className = curLang === 'kn' ? 'active' : '';
document.getElementById('knBtn').style.opacity = curLang === 'kn' ? '1' : '0.5';
document.querySelectorAll('.tl').forEach(el => {
if(!el.dataset.en) el.dataset.en = el.textContent; // Store original
el.textContent = curLang === 'kn' ? el.dataset.kn : el.dataset.en;
});
}

<!-- Admission Timeline -->
<div class="adm-timeline">
<h2>Admission Process</h2>
<div class="timeline-track">
<div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
<h4>Step 1 — NEET Qualification</h4>
<span>Appear for NEET-UG (BDS) or NEET-MDS (MDS) conducted by NTA / NBE.</span>
</div>
<div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
<h4>Step 2 — Counselling by RGUHS / KEA</h4>
<span>Attend state/central counselling. RRDCH participates via RGUHS round for Karnataka students.</span>
</div>
<div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
<h4>Step 3 — Document Verification</h4>
<span>Produce 10th, 12th, NEET scorecard, community certificate, and photographs at RRDCH admissions office.</span>
</div>
<div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
<h4>Step 4 — Fee Payment & Enrollment</h4>
<span>Complete fee payment, hostel booking, and receive your college ID and timetable.</span>
</div>
</div>
</div>

function calcWaitTime(waitingCount) {
let avg = parseInt(localStorage.getItem("avgTreatTime")) || 8;
return waitingCount * avg;
}
function showToast(msg) {
const t = document.getElementById("toast");
.textContent = msg; t.style.display = "block";
setTimeout(() => t.style.display = "none", 2000);
}
const sb = window.sb || (window.RRDCH_CONFIG && window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_URL && !window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_URL.startsWith("YOUR_")
? supabase.createClient(window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_URL, window.RRDCH_CONFIG.SUPABASE_ANON_KEY)
: null);

let curDoc = null;

const liveAlerts = [
{ token: 47, name: 'Priya Nair', reason: 'Crown Fitting' },
